## Plugin System Integration

`EditorNode` manages all editor plugins through multiple lists. Plugins can be built-in (compiled into the editor) or extension-based (loaded from addons).

### Plugin Registration Flow

```mermaid
graph TB
    Init[Editor Initialization]
    
    subgraph "Built-in Plugins"
        InitCB[plugin_init_callbacks]
        Create[create plugin instances]
        AddBuiltin[add_editor_plugin]
    end
    
    subgraph "Extension Plugins"
        LoadAddon[load addon from res://addons/]
        EnableAddon[set_addon_plugin_enabled]
        CreateExt[instantiate plugin script]
        AddExt[add_editor_plugin]
    end
    
    subgraph "EditorData"
        ED[editor_plugins vector]
        Notify[notify_edited_scene_changed]
    end
    
    Init --> InitCB
    InitCB --> Create
    Create --> AddBuiltin
    
    Init --> LoadAddon
    LoadAddon --> EnableAddon
    EnableAddon --> CreateExt
    CreateExt --> AddExt
    
    AddBuiltin --> ED
    AddExt --> ED
    
    ED --> Notify
```

Sources: [editor/editor_node.cpp:not shown but referenced in header](), [editor/editor_node.h:496-500](), [editor/editor_data.cpp:486-492]()

### Plugin Callback Dispatch

When editor state changes, `EditorNode` dispatches callbacks to all registered plugins:

| Callback | Trigger | Implementation |
|----------|---------|----------------|
| `edited_scene_changed()` | Scene tab switched | Iterate `editor_plugins`, call on each |
| `notify_scene_changed()` | Scene content modified | Iterate `editor_plugins`, call with root node |
| `notify_resource_saved()` | Resource saved to disk | Iterate `editor_plugins`, call with resource |
| `apply_changes()` | Before scene save/project run | Iterate `editor_plugins`, call on each |
| `get_state()` | Before scene save/tab switch | Iterate `editor_plugins`, collect state dictionaries |
| `set_state()` | After scene load/tab switch | Iterate `editor_plugins`, restore state dictionaries |

Sources: [editor/editor_data.cpp:360-395](), [doc/classes/EditorPlugin.xml:14-409]()

### Plugin State Persistence

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant EditorNode
    participant EditorData
    participant Plugin1
    participant Plugin2
    participant ConfigFile
    
    Note over EditorNode: User switches scene tab
    
    EditorNode->>EditorData: get_editor_plugin_states()
    EditorData->>Plugin1: get_state()
    Plugin1-->>EditorData: Dictionary state1
    EditorData->>Plugin2: get_state()
    Plugin2-->>EditorData: Dictionary state2
    EditorData-->>EditorNode: combined Dictionary
    
    EditorNode->>ConfigFile: save to editstate file
    
    Note over EditorNode: User switches back to scene
    
    EditorNode->>ConfigFile: load from editstate file
    ConfigFile-->>EditorNode: Dictionary states
    EditorNode->>EditorData: set_editor_plugin_states(states)
    EditorData->>Plugin1: set_state(state1)
    EditorData->>Plugin2: set_state(state2)
```

Sources: [editor/editor_data.cpp:316-358](), [doc/classes/EditorPlugin.xml:266-278](), [doc/classes/EditorPlugin.xml:385-396]()

---

## State Persistence

The editor persists multiple layers of state across sessions:

### Persistence Layers

| Layer | File | Content | Managed By |
|-------|------|---------|------------|
| **Editor Layout** | `editor_layout.cfg` | Window positions, dock visibility, UI state | `EditorNode::_save_editor_layout()` |
| **Scene States** | `<scene>.tscn.editstate` | Plugin states per scene, selection, camera position | `EditorNode::_save_editor_states()` |
| **Editor Settings** | `editor_settings-4.tres` | Global preferences, recent files, shortcuts | `EditorSettings` singleton |
| **Project Metadata** | `project.godot` | Enabled addons, main scene, display settings | `ProjectSettings` |

Sources: [editor/editor_node.cpp:not shown in excerpt but referenced]()

### Scene State Save/Load

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Save Sequence"
        SS[Scene Save Triggered]
        SEX[_save_external_resources]
        SES[_save_editor_states]
        GPS[get_editor_plugin_states]
        WCF[write ConfigFile]
    end
    
    subgraph "Load Sequence"
        SL[Scene Load Triggered]
        RCF[read ConfigFile]
        LPS[_load_editor_plugin_states_from_config]
        SPS[set_editor_plugin_states]
    end
    
    SS --> SEX
    SEX --> SES
    SES --> GPS
    GPS --> WCF
    
    SL --> RCF
    RCF --> LPS
    LPS --> SPS
```

When a scene is saved, `EditorNode` calls `_save_editor_states()` which collects plugin states via `EditorData::get_editor_plugin_states()` and writes them to a `.editstate` ConfigFile alongside the scene file.

Sources: [editor/editor_node.h:571-572](), [editor/editor_data.cpp:316-327]()

### History ID Management

Each `EditedScene` has a unique `history_id` used to isolate undo/redo history:

```mermaid
graph TB
    ES1[EditedScene index 0<br/>history_id: 1]
    ES2[EditedScene index 1<br/>history_id: 2]
    ES3[EditedScene index 2<br/>history_id: 3]
    
    URM[EditorUndoRedoManager]
    H1[History 1<br/>undo/redo stack]
    H2[History 2<br/>undo/redo stack]
    H3[History 3<br/>undo/redo stack]
    
    ES1 -.->|references| H1
    ES2 -.->|references| H2
    ES3 -.->|references| H3
    
    URM --> H1
    URM --> H2
    URM --> H3
```

The `history_id` is assigned in `EditorData::add_edited_scene()` by incrementing `last_created_scene`. When a scene is removed, its history is discarded via `EditorUndoRedoManager::discard_history()`.

Sources: [editor/editor_data.cpp:613-636](), [editor/editor_data.cpp:668-670](), [editor/editor_data.h:145]()

## Key Workflows

### Opening a Scene

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant User
    participant EditorNode
    participant EditorData
    participant ResourceLoader
    participant EditorUndoRedoManager
    participant Plugins
    
    User->>EditorNode: load_scene(path)
    EditorNode->>ResourceLoader: load(path)
    ResourceLoader-->>EditorNode: PackedScene
    EditorNode->>EditorNode: instantiate scene root
    
    EditorNode->>EditorData: add_edited_scene()
    EditorData->>EditorData: create EditedScene
    EditorData->>EditorData: assign history_id
    EditorData-->>EditorNode: scene index
    
    EditorNode->>EditorData: set_edited_scene_root(root)
    EditorData->>EditorData: store root in EditedScene
    
    EditorNode->>EditorNode: _load_editor_plugin_states_from_config
    EditorNode->>Plugins: set_state(saved_state)
    
    EditorNode->>EditorData: notify_edited_scene_changed()
    EditorData->>Plugins: edited_scene_changed()
    EditorData->>Plugins: notify_scene_changed(root)
```

Sources: [editor/editor_node.cpp:not shown in excerpt but structure referenced](), [editor/editor_data.cpp:613-636](), [editor/editor_data.cpp:794-808]()

### Switching Scene Tabs

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant User
    participant EditorNode
    participant EditorData
    participant EditorSelection
    participant Plugins
    
    User->>EditorNode: click scene tab
    EditorNode->>EditorNode: _set_current_scene(idx)
    
    EditorNode->>EditorData: get_editor_plugin_states()
    EditorData->>Plugins: get_state() from all
    Plugins-->>EditorData: state dictionaries
    EditorData-->>EditorNode: combined states
    EditorNode->>EditorNode: store in old EditedScene.editor_states
    
    EditorNode->>EditorData: set_edited_scene(idx)
    EditorData->>EditorData: current_edited_scene = idx
    
    EditorNode->>EditorData: restore_edited_scene_state()
    EditorData->>EditorSelection: clear and restore selection
    EditorData->>EditorNode: restored editor_states
    
    EditorNode->>EditorData: set_editor_plugin_states(states)
    EditorData->>Plugins: set_state() to all
    
    EditorNode->>EditorData: notify_edited_scene_changed()
    EditorData->>Plugins: edited_scene_changed()
    EditorData->>Plugins: notify_scene_changed(new_root)
```

Sources: [editor/editor_node.cpp:not shown in excerpt](), [editor/editor_data.cpp:779-808](), [editor/editor_data.cpp:335-358]()

### Plugin Initialization

```mermaid
graph TB
    Start[Editor Startup]
    
    subgraph "Callback Registration"
        Reg1[Plugin calls add_plugin_init_callback]
        Reg2[Callback stored in static array]
    end
    
    subgraph "EditorNode Construction"
        Init[EditorNode::EditorNode]
        InitPlugins[init_plugins]
        CallCB[call all plugin_init_callbacks]
        CreatePlugin[callbacks create plugin instances]
    end
    
    subgraph "Plugin Addition"
        AddPlug[add_editor_plugin]
        AddToData[EditorData::add_editor_plugin]
        EnterTree[plugin->_enter_tree]
    end
    
    Start --> Reg1
    Reg1 --> Reg2
    Start --> Init
    Init --> InitPlugins
    InitPlugins --> CallCB
    CallCB --> CreatePlugin
    CreatePlugin --> AddPlug
    AddPlug --> AddToData
    AddPlug --> EnterTree
```

Built-in plugins register callbacks via `EditorNode::add_plugin_init_callback()` which are stored in a static array. During `EditorNode::init_plugins()`, all callbacks are invoked to create plugin instances, which are then added via `add_editor_plugin()`.

Sources: [editor/editor_node.h:497-498](), [editor/editor_node.cpp:not shown in excerpt](), [editor/editor_data.cpp:490-492]()

---

## Summary

The editor core architecture is designed around a singleton orchestrator pattern:

- **EditorNode** is the central singleton that coordinates all editor operations and owns key subsystems
- **EditorData** manages the state of open scenes, plugin states, and provides scene switching logic
- **EditorInterface** provides a stable public API for plugins, decoupling them from EditorNode internals
- **EditorSelection** and **EditorSelectionHistory** track current selection and navigation history
- **Plugin System** uses callback dispatch to notify all plugins of editor state changes
- **State Persistence** uses per-scene `.editstate` files and a global `editor_layout.cfg` for saving editor state

This architecture enables extensibility through plugins while maintaining clean separation between core state management and plugin-specific logic.23:T4a19,# Editor Viewport Plugins

- [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml](doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml)
- [doc/classes/Node3DGizmo.xml](doc/classes/Node3DGizmo.xml)

</details>



## Purpose and Scope

Editor Viewport Plugins provide the interactive 2D and 3D scene editing capabilities in Godot's editor. This includes the `CanvasItemEditor` for 2D scene manipulation and the `Node3DEditor` for 3D scene editing, along with the gizmo system that enables visual manipulation tools for 3D nodes.

For information about the overall editor architecture and plugin registration, see [Editor Core: EditorNode and State Management](#4.1). For editor UI components like the Scene Tree and Inspector, see [Editor Docks: Scene Tree and File System](#4.3).

## Viewport Editor Architecture

The editor provides two primary viewport plugins that handle scene editing within the editor's viewport:

| Viewport Plugin | Purpose | Target Node Types |
|----------------|---------|------------------|
| `CanvasItemEditor` | 2D scene manipulation, handles positioning, rotation, scaling of CanvasItem nodes | CanvasItem, Node2D, Control |
| `Node3DEditor` | 3D scene manipulation, camera controls, gizmo management | Node3D and derivatives |

Both editors extend `EditorPlugin` and are registered with `EditorNode` during editor initialization. The viewport plugins integrate directly with the editor's viewport system to provide real-time visual feedback and manipulation capabilities.

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Editor Plugin System"
        EP["EditorPlugin<br/>(base class)"]
        EI["EditorInterface<br/>(public API)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Viewport Editors"
        CIE["CanvasItemEditor<br/>(2D editor)"]
        N3DE["Node3DEditor<br/>(3D editor)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "3D Gizmo System"
        N3DGP["EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin<br/>(gizmo plugin base)"]
        N3DG["EditorNode3DGizmo<br/>(gizmo instance)"]
        N3DGBase["Node3DGizmo<br/>(abstract base)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Scene Integration"
        Node3D["Node3D<br/>(3D scene nodes)"]
        CanvasItem["CanvasItem<br/>(2D scene nodes)"]
    end
    
    EP -->|"extends"| CIE
    EP -->|"extends"| N3DE
    EP -->|"extends"| N3DGP
    
    EI -->|"add_node_3d_gizmo_plugin()"| N3DGP
    
    N3DGP -->|"_create_gizmo()"| N3DG
    N3DG -->|"extends"| N3DGBase
    
    N3DE -->|"manages"| N3DGP
    N3DE -->|"edits"| Node3D
    CIE -->|"edits"| CanvasItem
    
    Node3D -->|"add_gizmo()"| N3DG
```

**Sources:** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:1-218](), [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:1-219](), [doc/classes/Node3DGizmo.xml:1-13]()

## 3D Gizmo Plugin System

The 3D gizmo system provides visual manipulation tools for Node3D objects in the editor. The system consists of three primary classes:

### Core Gizmo Classes

**`Node3DGizmo`** [doc/classes/Node3DGizmo.xml:1-13]()
- Abstract base class that connects Node3D scene nodes with editor-specific gizmos
- No exposed API; serves as the interface between the scene graph and editor tools
- Node3D nodes can have gizmos attached via `Node3D.add_gizmo()`

**`EditorNode3DGizmo`** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:1-219]()
- Concrete implementation providing the gizmo functionality
- Manages visual elements (meshes, lines, handles, billboards)
- Handles user interaction (handle dragging, subgizmo selection)
- Contains collision data for picking and selection

**`EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin`** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:1-219]()
- Factory and manager for gizmo types
- Defines which nodes get gizmos via `_has_gizmo()`
- Creates gizmo instances via `_create_gizmo()`
- Provides material management and gizmo configuration
- Implements the behavior for handle manipulation and subgizmo editing

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Plugin Registration Flow"
        Plugin["Custom EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin"]
        AddPlugin["EditorPlugin.add_node_3d_gizmo_plugin()"]
        N3DEditor["Node3DEditor<br/>(singleton)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Gizmo Creation Flow"
        HasGizmo["_has_gizmo(node)"]
        CreateGizmo["_create_gizmo(node)"]
        GizmoInstance["EditorNode3DGizmo instance"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Gizmo Lifecycle"
        Redraw["_redraw()"]
        AddVisuals["add_lines()<br/>add_mesh()<br/>add_handles()"]
        HandleEdit["_set_handle()"]
        Commit["_commit_handle()"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Node Integration"
        Node3DNode["Node3D node"]
        GizmoRef["node.add_gizmo()"]
    end
    
    Plugin -->|"registered via"| AddPlugin
    AddPlugin -->|"registers with"| N3DEditor
    
    N3DEditor -->|"checks"| HasGizmo
    HasGizmo -->|"if true"| CreateGizmo
    CreateGizmo -->|"returns"| GizmoInstance
    
    GizmoInstance -->|"attached to"| Node3DNode
    Node3DNode -->|"stores via"| GizmoRef
    
    GizmoInstance -->|"triggered on changes"| Redraw
    Redraw -->|"calls"| AddVisuals
    
    AddVisuals -->|"enables"| HandleEdit
    HandleEdit -->|"on mouse release"| Commit
```

**Sources:** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:1-218](), [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:1-219](), [doc/classes/Node3DGizmo.xml:1-13]()

## Gizmo Plugin Lifecycle

The gizmo plugin lifecycle involves several key phases from plugin registration to interactive editing:

### Registration Phase

Plugins are registered using `EditorPlugin.add_node_3d_gizmo_plugin()` [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:8](), typically in the editor plugin's `_enter_tree()` method. The `Node3DEditor` singleton maintains a registry of all registered gizmo plugins.

### Node Assignment Phase

When a Node3D is added to the scene tree in the editor:

1. `Node3DEditor` iterates through all registered gizmo plugins
2. Each plugin's `_has_gizmo(node)` method is called [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:101-106]()
3. If the method returns `true`, `_create_gizmo(node)` is called [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:53-58]()
4. The created `EditorNode3DGizmo` instance is attached to the node
5. Priority is determined by `_get_priority()` [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:86-91]()

### Redraw Phase

The `_redraw()` method is called whenever the gizmo needs to update its visual representation [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:123-128]():

**Common redraw pattern:**
1. Call `gizmo.clear()` to remove previous visual elements [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:172-176]()
2. Add new visual elements based on node properties:
   - `add_lines()` for line-based visualizations [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:143-151]()
   - `add_mesh()` for mesh visualizations [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:153-161]()
   - `add_handles()` for interactive manipulation points [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:130-141]()
   - `add_unscaled_billboard()` for icons [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:163-170]()
3. Add collision geometry for picking:
   - `add_collision_segments()` [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:116-121]()
   - `add_collision_triangles()` [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:123-128]()

**Sources:** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:53-58](), [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:101-106](), [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:123-128](), [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:143-176]()

## Handle System

Handles provide interactive manipulation points for editing node properties directly in the 3D viewport. The handle system supports both primary and secondary handles with different selection priorities.

### Handle Types

**Primary Handles** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:130-141]()
- Default handles with normal selection priority
- Added via `add_handles()` with `secondary = false`

**Secondary Handles** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:130-141]()
- Lower priority handles that can share positions with primary handles
- When holding Shift, secondary handles gain higher priority
- Added via `add_handles()` with `secondary = true`

### Handle Editing Flow

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Handle Interaction Sequence"
        MouseDown["User clicks handle"]
        BeginAction["_begin_handle_action(id, secondary)"]
        GetValue["_get_handle_value(id, secondary)"]
        StoreRestore["Store restore value"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Dragging Phase"
        MouseMove["User drags mouse"]
        SetHandle["_set_handle(id, secondary, camera, screen_pos)"]
        UpdateNode["Update node properties"]
        VisualFeedback["Visual feedback via _redraw()"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Commit Phase"
        MouseRelease["User releases mouse"]
        CommitHandle["_commit_handle(id, secondary, restore, cancel)"]
        CreateUndo["Create UndoRedo action"]
        FinalRedraw["Final _redraw()"]
    end
    
    MouseDown --> BeginAction
    BeginAction --> GetValue
    GetValue --> StoreRestore
    
    StoreRestore --> MouseMove
    MouseMove --> SetHandle
    SetHandle --> UpdateNode
    UpdateNode --> VisualFeedback
    VisualFeedback -->|"continues"| MouseMove
    
    MouseMove --> MouseRelease
    MouseRelease --> CommitHandle
    CommitHandle --> CreateUndo
    CreateUndo --> FinalRedraw
```

### Handle Callback Methods

| Method | Phase | Purpose |
|--------|-------|---------|
| `_begin_handle_action()` [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:14-21]() | Start | Called when handle editing begins |
| `_get_handle_value()` [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:75-84]() | Start | Returns current value to use as "restore" for undo |
| `_get_handle_name()` [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:66-73]() | Display | Returns handle name for user reference |
| `_set_handle()` [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:130-141]() | Dragging | Updates node properties during drag, receives camera and screen position |
| `_is_handle_highlighted()` [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:108-115]() | Display | Returns whether handle should be highlighted |
| `_commit_handle()` [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:28-40]() | Commit | Creates UndoRedo action with current value as "do" and restore value as "undo" |

**Cancel behavior:** If `cancel = true` in `_commit_handle()`, the restore value should be applied directly without creating an UndoRedo action [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:37]().

**Sources:** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:14-141](), [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:130-141]()

## Subgizmo System

Subgizmos enable selection and transformation of sub-elements within a node, such as individual points in a Path3D or bones in a skeleton. Each subgizmo is identified by a unique integer ID.

### Subgizmo Selection

**Ray Intersection Selection** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:161-168]()
- Method: `_subgizmos_intersect_ray(gizmo, camera, screen_pos)`
- Returns: Single subgizmo ID that should be selected at the screen position
- Used for: Click selection

**Frustum Selection** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:152-159]()
- Method: `_subgizmos_intersect_frustum(gizmo, camera, frustum_planes)`
- Returns: Array of subgizmo IDs contained within the frustum
- Used for: Box/drag selection

### Subgizmo Transform Editing

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Subgizmo Selection"
        Click["User clicks in viewport"]
        RayTest["_subgizmos_intersect_ray()"]
        SelectSubgizmo["Select subgizmo by ID"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Transform Editing"
        Transform["User manipulates transform gizmo"]
        GetTransform["_get_subgizmo_transform(id)"]
        SetTransform["_set_subgizmo_transform(id, transform)"]
        NodeUpdate["Update node data"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Commit"
        Release["User completes transformation"]
        CommitSubgizmos["_commit_subgizmos(ids, restores, cancel)"]
        UndoRedo["Create UndoRedo action"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Visual Update"
        Redraw["_redraw()"]
        GetSelection["get_subgizmo_selection()"]
        Highlight["Highlight selected subgizmos"]
    end
    
    Click --> RayTest
    RayTest --> SelectSubgizmo
    
    SelectSubgizmo --> Transform
    Transform --> GetTransform
    GetTransform --> SetTransform
    SetTransform --> NodeUpdate
    NodeUpdate --> Redraw
    
    Transform --> Release
    Release --> CommitSubgizmos
    CommitSubgizmos --> UndoRedo
    
    Redraw --> GetSelection
    GetSelection --> Highlight
```

### Subgizmo Callback Methods

| Method | Purpose | Transform Space |
|--------|---------|----------------|
| `_subgizmos_intersect_ray()` [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:161-168]() | Returns subgizmo ID at screen position | N/A |
| `_subgizmos_intersect_frustum()` [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:152-159]() | Returns subgizmo IDs within frustum | N/A |
| `_get_subgizmo_transform()` [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:93-99]() | Returns current transform for undo | Local space relative to Node3D |
| `_set_subgizmo_transform()` [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:143-150]() | Updates subgizmo during editing | Local space relative to Node3D |
| `_commit_subgizmos()` [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:42-51]() | Creates UndoRedo action for transform changes | Local space relative to Node3D |

**Query methods for highlighting:**
- `get_subgizmo_selection()` [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:190-194]() - Returns array of selected subgizmo IDs
- `is_subgizmo_selected(id)` [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:196-201]() - Checks if specific subgizmo is selected

**Sources:** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:42-168](), [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:190-201]()

## Material System

Gizmo plugins manage materials for rendering gizmo visual elements. Materials can have variants for different gizmo states (normal, selected, editable).

### Material Creation Methods

**`create_material(name, color, billboard, on_top, use_vertex_color)`** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:198-207]()
- Creates unshaded material with selected/editable variants
- Used with `add_mesh()` and `add_lines()`
- Parameters control rendering behavior (billboarding, depth testing, vertex colors)

**`create_icon_material(name, texture, on_top, color)`** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:188-196]()
- Creates billboard material with texture
- Used with `add_unscaled_billboard()`
- Generates selected/editable variants with modified colors

**`create_handle_material(name, billboard, texture)`** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:178-186]()
- Creates material specifically for handles
- Generates selected/editable variants
- Optional custom texture, defaults to editor handle icon

**`add_material(name, material)`** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:170-176]()
- Adds custom material to internal registry
- For advanced use cases requiring specific material setup

### Material Retrieval

**`get_material(name, gizmo)`** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:209-215]()
- Retrieves material by name from internal registry
- If gizmo is provided, returns appropriate variant based on gizmo state:
  - Normal variant for inactive gizmos
  - Selected variant for selected gizmos
  - Editable variant for active editing gizmos

### Material Usage Pattern

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "Material Creation (in plugin constructor)"
        CreateMat["create_material('lines', color)"]
        CreateHandle["create_handle_material('handles')"]
        CreateIcon["create_icon_material('icon', texture)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Material Storage"
        Registry["Internal material registry"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Material Retrieval (in _redraw)"
        GetMat["get_material('lines', gizmo)"]
        GetHandle["get_material('handles', gizmo)"]
        Variant["Returns state-appropriate variant"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Visual Element Creation"
        AddLines["add_lines(points, material)"]
        AddHandles["add_handles(points, material)"]
        AddBillboard["add_unscaled_billboard(material)"]
    end
    
    CreateMat --> Registry
    CreateHandle --> Registry
    CreateIcon --> Registry
    
    Registry --> GetMat
    Registry --> GetHandle
    GetMat --> Variant
    GetHandle --> Variant
    
    Variant --> AddLines
    Variant --> AddHandles
    Variant --> AddBillboard
```

**Sources:** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:170-215]()

## Gizmo Visibility and Priority

Gizmos can be shown, hidden, and prioritized to control their behavior in the editor.

### Visibility Control

**`_can_be_hidden()`** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:22-26]()
- Returns whether gizmos from this plugin can be hidden via the gizmo menu
- Default: `true`

**`_is_selectable_when_hidden()`** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:117-121]()
- Returns whether nodes with this gizmo can be selected when gizmo is hidden
- Allows selection without visual gizmo feedback

**`set_hidden(hidden)`** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:203-208]()
- Controls individual gizmo visibility
- Can be called at runtime to show/hide specific gizmos

### Priority System

**`_get_priority()`** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:86-91]()
- Determines selection and input handling priority
- Higher priority gizmos process inputs first
- Built-in editor gizmos return `-1`
- Default for custom plugins: `0` (higher than built-in)
- Used when multiple gizmos handle the same input

### Gizmo Naming

**`_get_gizmo_name()`** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:60-64]()
- Returns name displayed in the gizmo visibility menu
- Allows users to toggle gizmo types on/off

**Sources:** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:22-91](), [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:203-208]()

## Integration Summary

The viewport plugin system integrates tightly with the editor architecture:

| Component | Integration Point | Purpose |
|-----------|------------------|---------|
| `EditorPlugin` | Base class for all plugins | Provides registration mechanism via `add_node_3d_gizmo_plugin()` |
| `EditorInterface` | Public editor API | Exposes plugin registration to custom editor plugins |
| `Node3DEditor` | 3D viewport singleton | Manages gizmo plugin registry, creates gizmos for nodes |
| `CanvasItemEditor` | 2D viewport singleton | Handles 2D scene manipulation and editing |
| `Node3D` | Scene graph nodes | Receives and stores gizmo instances via `add_gizmo()` |
| `EditorUndoRedoManager` | History system | Integrates with handle/subgizmo commit for undo/redo |
| `Camera3D` | Viewport camera | Provided to handle/subgizmo methods for raycast calculations |

The gizmo system enables extensible, type-safe manipulation tools that integrate seamlessly with the editor's undo/redo system and provide immediate visual feedback during editing operations.

**Sources:** [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmoPlugin.xml:1-218](), [doc/classes/EditorNode3DGizmo.xml:1-219](), [doc/classes/Node3DGizmo.xml:1-13]()24:T4d6a,# Editor Docks: Scene Tree and File System

This document describes the Scene Tree Dock and File System Dock, two fundamental editor UI components that provide scene hierarchy management and project asset browsing respectively. For information about other editor docks like the Inspector Dock, see [Editor Core: EditorNode and State Management](#4.1).

## Overview

The editor docks are persistent UI panels that provide access to core editing functionality. The Scene Tree Dock and File System Dock are among the most frequently used, appearing in the default editor layout and integrating deeply with the scene editing workflow.

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Editor Core"
        EN["EditorNode<br/>(Central Orchestrator)"]
        EI["EditorInterface<br/>(Public API)"]
        ED["EditorData<br/>(State Management)"]
        ESel["EditorSelection<br/>(Selection Tracking)"]
        EURM["EditorUndoRedoManager<br/>(History)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Scene Tree Dock"
        STD["SceneTreeDock"]
        SceneTreeEditor["SceneTreeEditor<br/>(Tree UI)"]
        NodeMenu["Node Context Menu"]
    end
    
    subgraph "File System Dock"
        FSD["FileSystemDock"]
        FileTree["FileSystem Tree/List UI"]
        FileMenu["File Context Menu"]
        EFS["EditorFileSystem<br/>(Asset Scanner)"]
        ERP["EditorResourcePreview<br/>(Thumbnails)"]
    end
    
    EN -->|"creates and owns"| STD
    EN -->|"creates and owns"| FSD
    EN -->|"provides"| EI
    
    EI -->|"get_file_system_dock()"| FSD
    
    STD -->|"uses"| ESel
    STD -->|"uses"| EURM
    STD -->|"contains"| SceneTreeEditor
    STD -->|"displays"| NodeMenu
    
    FSD -->|"uses"| EFS
    FSD -->|"uses"| ERP
    FSD -->|"contains"| FileTree
    FSD -->|"displays"| FileMenu
    
    STD -->|"modifies"| ED
    FSD -->|"loads resources via"| ResourceLoader["ResourceLoader"]
```

**Diagram: Editor Docks Architecture**

Sources: [editor/editor_node.h:1-900](), [editor/editor_node.cpp:58-65](), [editor/editor_interface.h:1-200]()

## Scene Tree Dock

The `SceneTreeDock` class provides the primary interface for viewing and manipulating the node hierarchy of the currently edited scene. It displays a tree view of all nodes in the scene and provides context menus and operations for node management.

### Core Responsibilities

| Responsibility | Implementation |
|---|---|
| **Hierarchy Display** | Uses `SceneTreeEditor` to render the tree view of nodes |
| **Node Operations** | Create, delete, duplicate, reparent nodes via context menu |
| **Selection Management** | Integrates with `EditorSelection` to track selected nodes |
| **Undo/Redo** | All operations use `EditorUndoRedoManager` for history |
| **Scene Editing** | Modify node properties, groups, and connections |

### Key Integration Points

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "Scene Editing Workflow"
        User["User Interaction"]
        STD["SceneTreeDock"]
        STE["SceneTreeEditor"]
        ESel["EditorSelection"]
        EURM["EditorUndoRedoManager"]
        ED["EditorData"]
        SceneRoot["Scene Root Node"]
    end
    
    User -->|"selects node"| STE
    STE -->|"updates"| ESel
    ESel -->|"notifies"| STD
    
    User -->|"modifies hierarchy"| STD
    STD -->|"creates action"| EURM
    EURM -->|"modifies"| SceneRoot
    
    STD -->|"reads/writes state"| ED
    ED -->|"stores edited scenes"| EditedScene["EditedScene struct"]
```

**Diagram: Scene Tree Dock Data Flow**

The Scene Tree Dock is created during editor initialization and persists throughout the editor session:

- Created in [editor/editor_node.cpp:58-65]() where `SceneTreeDock` is included
- Accessed via `EditorInterface::get_singleton()` methods
- Communicates with `EditorSelection` to coordinate selected nodes with other editor components

Sources: [editor/editor_node.h:1-900](), [editor/editor_data.h:1-200](), [editor/editor_data.cpp:1-900]()

### Node Selection and Editing

The Scene Tree Dock maintains tight integration with the editor's selection system:

```mermaid
graph TB
    TreeClick["User clicks node in tree"]
    STDSelect["SceneTreeDock processes selection"]
    ESelUpdate["EditorSelection::add_node() or clear()"]
    Inspector["InspectorDock updates"]
    Viewport["Viewport highlights selection"]
    HistoryAdd["EditorSelectionHistory::add_object()"]
    
    TreeClick --> STDSelect
    STDSelect --> ESelUpdate
    ESelUpdate --> Inspector
    ESelUpdate --> Viewport
    ESelUpdate --> HistoryAdd
```

**Diagram: Node Selection Flow**

When a node is selected in the Scene Tree Dock:
1. The `SceneTreeEditor` detects the click/selection change
2. `EditorSelection` is updated with the new selection
3. The Inspector Dock is notified to display node properties
4. The 2D/3D viewport highlights the selected node(s)
5. Selection history is updated for navigation

Sources: [editor/editor_data.cpp:49-256](), [editor/editor_node.h:260-290]()

### Undo/Redo Integration

All node hierarchy modifications go through the undo/redo system:

| Operation | Implementation |
|---|---|
| **Add Node** | Creates undo action with `add_child()` do/undo methods |
| **Delete Node** | Stores node state before deletion for restoration |
| **Reparent Node** | Records old and new parent relationships |
| **Duplicate Node** | Clones node with sub-resources, records in history |
| **Property Change** | Captured via `EditorUndoRedoManager` inspector hooks |

The undo/redo manager maintains separate history stacks for each edited scene, identified by a history ID stored in `EditorData::EditedScene`:

Sources: [editor/editor_data.h:113-126](), [editor/editor_data.cpp:418-457]()

## File System Dock

The `FileSystemDock` class provides the file browser interface for the project, displaying all resources and files in the `res://` directory. It handles asset operations, import management, and resource preview generation.

### Core Components

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "FileSystemDock Components"
        FSD["FileSystemDock<br/>(Main Dock Class)"]
        TreeView["Tree View<br/>(Folder Navigation)"]
        ListView["List View<br/>(File Display)"]
        PathBar["Path Navigation Bar"]
        FilterBox["Search/Filter Input"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Backend Services"
        EFS["EditorFileSystem<br/>(Scans project files)"]
        ERP["EditorResourcePreview<br/>(Generates thumbnails)"]
        RL["ResourceLoader<br/>(Loads resources)"]
        ImportSystem["Import System<br/>(Processes assets)"]
    end
    
    FSD --> TreeView
    FSD --> ListView
    FSD --> PathBar
    FSD --> FilterBox
    
    FSD -->|"queries file structure"| EFS
    FSD -->|"requests thumbnails"| ERP
    FSD -->|"loads on double-click"| RL
    EFS -->|"triggers"| ImportSystem
    
    EFS -.->|"signals updates"| FSD
    ERP -.->|"returns previews"| FSD
```

**Diagram: File System Dock Architecture**

Sources: [editor/editor_node.cpp:59](), [doc/classes/EditorInterface.xml:164-170]()

### Asset Scanning and Import System

The File System Dock relies on `EditorFileSystem` to maintain an up-to-date view of the project directory:

| Service | Responsibility |
|---|---|
| **EditorFileSystem** | Scans `res://` directory, detects file changes, manages `.import` files |
| **EditorResourcePreview** | Generates thumbnail images for resources asynchronously |
| **ResourceImporter** | Processes raw assets (images, audio, 3D models) into engine formats |
| **ResourceLoader** | Loads resources when files are opened or dragged into the scene |

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant User
    participant FSD as FileSystemDock
    participant EFS as EditorFileSystem
    participant RI as ResourceImporter
    participant RL as ResourceLoader
    participant Cache as ResourceCache
    
    User->>FSD: Drag file into project
    FSD->>EFS: File added to filesystem
    EFS->>EFS: Scan and detect new file
    EFS->>RI: Check if import needed
    RI->>RI: Process asset (.png -> .ctex)
    RI->>EFS: Import complete, .import file created
    EFS-->>FSD: Signal filesystem_changed
    FSD->>FSD: Refresh file list
    
    User->>FSD: Double-click resource
    FSD->>RL: load(path)
    RL->>Cache: Check cache
    alt Resource cached
        Cache-->>FSD: Return cached resource
    else Not cached
        RL->>RL: Load from disk
        RL->>Cache: Store in cache
        Cache-->>FSD: Return new resource
    end
```

**Diagram: File Import and Loading Workflow**

Sources: [core/io/resource_loader.cpp:275-333](), [core/io/resource_loader.h:105-250](), [core/io/resource_importer.cpp:1-500]()

### Resource Loading Workflow

When a file is opened from the File System Dock, the following process occurs:

1. **Path Validation**: The file path is validated using `ResourceLoader::_validate_local_path()` at [core/io/resource_loader.cpp:477-486]()
2. **Format Detection**: The loader iterates through registered `ResourceFormatLoader` instances to find one that recognizes the file extension
3. **Cache Check**: `ResourceCache` is queried to see if the resource is already loaded at [core/io/resource_loader.cpp:588-598]()
4. **Loading**: If not cached, the appropriate format loader reads the file (text-based via `ResourceLoaderText` or binary via `ResourceLoaderBinary`)
5. **Registration**: The loaded resource is registered in the cache and assigned its path

For imported resources (e.g., `.png` images), the system loads the processed `.ctex` file from `.godot/imported/` rather than the original source file.

Sources: [core/io/resource_loader.cpp:513-642](), [core/io/resource_format_binary.cpp:1-1500](), [scene/resources/resource_format_text.cpp:1-1500]()

### File Operations

The File System Dock supports standard file management operations:

| Operation | Implementation |
|---|---|
| **Move/Rename** | Updates resource paths, renames `.import` files, updates dependencies |
| **Delete** | Removes file and associated `.import` file, checks for dependencies |
| **Duplicate** | Copies file and creates new `.import` file if needed |
| **Create Folder** | Creates directory in project filesystem |
| **Import/Re-import** | Triggers `ResourceImporter` to process the file with current settings |

```mermaid
graph TD
    UserDelete["User deletes file"]
    CheckDeps["Check dependencies"]
    HasDeps{Has dependencies?}
    ShowWarning["Show dependency warning dialog"]
    UserConfirm{User confirms?}
    DeleteFile["Delete file from disk"]
    DeleteImport["Delete .import file"]
    UpdateCache["Update ResourceCache"]
    NotifyEFS["Notify EditorFileSystem"]
    Refresh["Refresh FileSystemDock display"]
    
    UserDelete --> CheckDeps
    CheckDeps --> HasDeps
    HasDeps -->|Yes| ShowWarning
    HasDeps -->|No| DeleteFile
    ShowWarning --> UserConfirm
    UserConfirm -->|Yes| DeleteFile
    UserConfirm -->|No| Refresh
    DeleteFile --> DeleteImport
    DeleteImport --> UpdateCache
    UpdateCache --> NotifyEFS
    NotifyEFS --> Refresh
```

**Diagram: File Deletion Workflow**

Dependency checking is performed by examining all resources in the project to see if they reference the file being deleted. This prevents breaking scene files or other resources that depend on the asset.

Sources: [editor/editor_node.cpp:410-411](), [core/io/resource_loader.cpp:184-192]()

## Integration with EditorNode

Both docks are created and managed by `EditorNode`, the central editor orchestrator:

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "EditorNode Initialization"
        Init["EditorNode::_notification(NOTIFICATION_READY)"]
        CreateDocks["Create dock instances"]
        STDCreate["SceneTreeDock* scene_tree_dock = memnew(SceneTreeDock)"]
        FSDCreate["FileSystemDock* filesystem_dock = memnew(FileSystemDock)"]
        AddToDockMgr["Add to EditorDockManager"]
        ConnectSignals["Connect dock signals to EditorNode"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Dock Manager"
        EDM["EditorDockManager"]
        DockSlots["Dock slot containers"]
        Layout["Save/Load dock layout"]
    end
    
    Init --> CreateDocks
    CreateDocks --> STDCreate
    CreateDocks --> FSDCreate
    STDCreate --> AddToDockMgr
    FSDCreate --> AddToDockMgr
    AddToDockMgr --> EDM
    EDM --> DockSlots
    CreateDocks --> ConnectSignals
    EDM --> Layout
```

**Diagram: Dock Initialization in EditorNode**

The docks are accessible through the `EditorInterface` singleton:
- `EditorInterface::get_file_system_dock()` returns the `FileSystemDock` instance
- The Scene Tree Dock is accessed indirectly through scene editing operations

Sources: [editor/editor_node.cpp:1-900](), [editor/editor_interface.cpp:1-500](), [doc/classes/EditorInterface.xml:164-170]()

### Dock Persistence and Layout

The editor saves dock positions and states in the editor layout configuration:

| Configuration | Storage Location |
|---|---|
| **Dock Positions** | Editor layout `.cfg` files in user config directory |
| **Split Ratios** | Saved in layout under dock slot keys |
| **Visibility State** | Tracked per dock in layout configuration |
| **Scene-Specific State** | Stored in `EditorData::EditedScene` for scene tree state |

When the editor loads a layout, it restores dock positions by calling methods on `EditorDockManager`, which repositions the dock containers according to the saved configuration.

Sources: [editor/editor_node.h:388-391](), [editor/editor_data.h:113-126]()

## Resource Preview System

The File System Dock uses `EditorResourcePreview` to generate thumbnails for resources displayed in list view:

```mermaid
graph LR
    FSD["FileSystemDock"]
    ERP["EditorResourcePreview"]
    Plugins["Preview Generator Plugins"]
    Queue["Preview Queue"]
    Thread["Background Thread"]
    Cache["Thumbnail Cache"]
    
    FSD -->|"queue_resource_preview(path)"| ERP
    ERP -->|"add to queue"| Queue
    Queue -->|"process"| Thread
    Thread -->|"select generator"| Plugins
    Plugins -->|"generate thumbnail"| Thread
    Thread -->|"save to cache"| Cache
    Cache -.->|"callback with texture"| FSD
    FSD -->|"update icon"| FileListItem["File List Item"]
```

**Diagram: Resource Preview Generation**

Preview generation is asynchronous to avoid blocking the editor UI. The system:
1. Queues preview requests as files become visible in the File System Dock
2. Processes them on a background thread using registered preview generator plugins
3. Caches the generated thumbnails
4. Calls back to the File System Dock with the thumbnail texture when ready

Different resource types have specialized preview generators (e.g., `EditorTexturePreviewPlugin` for images, `EditorScenePreviewPlugin` for 3D scenes).

Sources: [editor/editor_node.cpp:111](), [doc/classes/EditorInterface.xml:1-400]()

## Common Operations

### Creating a New Scene

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant User
    participant Menu as File Menu
    participant EN as EditorNode
    participant ED as EditorData
    participant STD as SceneTreeDock
    
    User->>Menu: File > New Scene
    Menu->>EN: _menu_option(SCENE_NEW_SCENE)
    EN->>ED: add_edited_scene()
    ED->>ED: Create new EditedScene entry
    EN->>STD: Update tree to show empty scene
    STD->>STD: Clear tree view
    EN->>EN: _update_title()
    
    Note over User,STD: Scene is empty, ready for nodes
```

**Diagram: New Scene Creation Flow**

Sources: [editor/editor_node.h:143-163](), [editor/editor_data.cpp:600-900]()

### Opening a Scene File

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant User
    participant FSD as FileSystemDock
    participant EN as EditorNode
    participant RL as ResourceLoader
    participant Cache as ResourceCache
    participant ED as EditorData
    
    User->>FSD: Double-click .tscn file
    FSD->>EN: load_scene(path)
    EN->>RL: load(path, "PackedScene")
    RL->>Cache: Check cache
    alt In cache
        Cache-->>RL: Return cached PackedScene
    else Not in cache
        RL->>RL: Parse .tscn file
        RL->>Cache: Register resource
        Cache-->>RL: Return PackedScene
    end
    RL-->>EN: Return PackedScene
    EN->>EN: set_edited_scene(scene.instantiate())
    EN->>ED: Update edited scene data
    EN->>EN: Notify plugins via edited_scene_changed()
```

**Diagram: Scene File Loading**

When a scene file is double-clicked in the File System Dock, it goes through the complete resource loading pipeline, including parsing external resource dependencies and sub-resources defined in the scene file.

Sources: [editor/editor_node.cpp:275-333](), [scene/resources/resource_format_text.cpp:184-421]()

### Filtering Files

The File System Dock provides a search/filter box that filters the displayed files:

1. User types in filter box
2. FileSystemDock applies filter to file list
3. Only files matching the filter (by name or type) are shown
4. The shortcut `Ctrl+Shift+F` (or `ED_IS_SHORTCUT("editor/filter_files")`) focuses the filter box

This is implemented at [editor/editor_node.cpp:410-411]() where the shortcut is registered and handled.

Sources: [editor/editor_node.cpp:404-460](), [doc/classes/EditorInterface.xml:73-77]()

## Extension Points

Both docks can be extended or integrated with via `EditorPlugin`:

| Extension Type | Method | Description |
|---|---|
| **Custom Import Plugin** | `EditorImportPlugin` | Add support for new file formats in File System Dock |
| **Resource Preview Plugin** | `EditorResourcePreviewGenerator` | Generate custom thumbnails for resources |
| **File Dialog Integration** | `EditorFileDialog` | Use editor's file browser in plugin dialogs |
| **Scene Tree Manipulation** | `EditorInterface::get_edited_scene_root()` | Access and modify the current scene programmatically |

Plugins can access the File System Dock via `EditorInterface::get_file_system_dock()` to programmatically navigate to files or trigger operations.

Sources: [doc/classes/EditorPlugin.xml:1-1000](), [doc/classes/EditorInterface.xml:1-400](), [editor/editor_interface.cpp:1-500]()25:T5ec5,# Editor Settings and Debugging

## Overview

This document covers the editor configuration system and runtime debugging infrastructure in Godot. The **EditorSettings** class manages all project-independent editor preferences, while **SceneDebugger** provides live editing and runtime inspection capabilities for running games. For information about editor core orchestration, see [4.1](#4.1). For viewport editor plugins, see [4.2](#4.2).

The settings system controls editor behavior including viewport navigation, visual appearance, debugger limits, and keyboard shortcuts. The debugging system enables real-time scene modification, node inspection, and in-game selection through the **RuntimeNodeSelect** subsystem.

Sources: [editor/settings/editor_settings.h](), [scene/debugger/scene_debugger.h](), [doc/classes/EditorSettings.xml:1-30]()

## EditorSettings Architecture

### Storage and Lifecycle

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "EditorSettings Class"
        ES["EditorSettings<br/>Singleton"]
        Props["props: HashMap<String, VariantContainer>"]
        Hints["hints: HashMap<String, PropertyInfo>"]
        Shortcuts["shortcuts: HashMap<String, Ref<Shortcut>>"]
        Changed["changed_settings: HashSet<String>"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Storage"
        ConfigFile["editor_settings-4.tres<br/>ConfigFile"]
        Metadata["Project Metadata<br/>editor_settings-4.tres"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Access Points"
        EI["EditorInterface::get_editor_settings()"]
        Macro["EDITOR_GET() macro"]
        DirectSet["set_setting() / get_setting()"]
    end
    
    ES -->|"contains"| Props
    ES -->|"contains"| Hints
    ES -->|"contains"| Shortcuts
    ES -->|"tracks changes"| Changed
    
    ES -->|"saves to"| ConfigFile
    ES -->|"stores project data"| Metadata
    
    EI -->|"returns"| ES
    Macro -->|"accesses"| ES
    DirectSet -->|"modifies"| ES
    
    Props -->|"PropertyInfo metadata"| Hints
    Changed -->|"tracked on _set()"| Props
```

**EditorSettings Storage Model**

The `EditorSettings` class manages a central registry of editor preferences stored in `editor_settings-4.tres`. Each setting has:
- A **value** stored in the `props` HashMap as a `VariantContainer`
- Optional **PropertyInfo** metadata in `hints` for UI presentation
- An **initial** (default) value for reset functionality
- A **save** flag indicating whether to persist changes

Settings are accessed through `EditorInterface::get_editor_settings()` or the `EDITOR_GET()` macro. Changes are tracked in `changed_settings` and saved automatically when modified.

Sources: [editor/settings/editor_settings.h:76-150](), [editor/settings/editor_settings.cpp:73-100](), [editor/settings/editor_settings.cpp:102-167]()

### Setting Registration and Initialization

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "Initialization Flow"
        Load["_load_defaults()"]
        Initial["_initial_set()"]
        AddHint["add_property_hint()"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Setting Components"
        Value["Setting Value"]
        Default["Default Value"]
        Meta["PropertyInfo Hint"]
        Basic["Basic Setting Flag"]
    end
    
    Load -->|"calls for each setting"| Initial
    Initial -->|"sets value"| Value
    Initial -->|"stores"| Default
    Initial -->|"marks"| Basic
    Load -->|"registers"| AddHint
    AddHint -->|"defines UI"| Meta
    
    Value -->|"user modifiable"| Changed["Changed on Edit"]
    Default -->|"used for revert"| Revert["Revert Button"]
```

**Setting Initialization Process**

Settings are initialized in `_load_defaults()` using the `EDITOR_SETTING` macro pattern:

```cpp
// From editor/settings/editor_settings.cpp:407-456
EDITOR_SETTING(Variant::BOOL, PROPERTY_HINT_NONE, 
    "debugger/auto_switch_to_remote_scene_tree", false, "")
```

This creates the setting with:
1. **Type and hint**: Defines the data type and property hint for the inspector
2. **Default value**: Stored as `initial` for reset functionality  
3. **Hint string**: Additional metadata for enum options or range constraints

The `EDITOR_SETTING_BASIC` variant marks frequently-used settings for prominence in the settings UI.

Sources: [editor/settings/editor_settings.cpp:407-456](), [editor/settings/editor_settings.cpp:268-273]()

### Property System Integration

The `EditorSettings` class uses Godot's property system through `_get()`, `_set()`, and `_get_property_list()` overrides:

| Method | Purpose |
|--------|---------|
| `_set()` | Updates setting value, marks as changed, triggers `settings_changed` signal |
| `_get()` | Retrieves setting value or serializes shortcuts/builtin_action_overrides |
| `_get_property_list()` | Dynamically generates property list for inspector display |

Special handling exists for `shortcuts` and `builtin_action_overrides` which serialize to/from arrays for persistence.

Sources: [editor/settings/editor_settings.cpp:73-100](), [editor/settings/editor_settings.cpp:169-266](), [editor/settings/editor_settings.cpp:286-345]()

## Debugger Settings Configuration

### Debugger-Specific Settings

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Debugger Settings Categories"
        AutoSwitch["debugger/auto_switch_to_remote_scene_tree<br/>bool: Auto-switch to remote tree"]
        StackTrace["debugger/auto_switch_to_stack_trace<br/>bool: Show stack on breakpoint"]
        MaxNodes["debugger/max_node_selection<br/>int: Remote node selection limit"]
        ProfileNative["debugger/profile_native_calls<br/>bool: Profile engine methods"]
        FrameHistory["debugger/profiler_frame_history_size<br/>int: Profiler frame buffer"]
        MaxFunctions["debugger/profiler_frame_max_functions<br/>int: Function display limit"]
        TargetFPS["debugger/profiler_target_fps<br/>int: Visual profiler target"]
        InspectInterval["debugger/remote_inspect_refresh_interval<br/>float: Property refresh rate"]
        SceneInterval["debugger/remote_scene_tree_refresh_interval<br/>float: Tree refresh rate"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Used By"
        RemoteTree["Remote Scene Tree"]
        Profiler["EditorProfiler"]
        Inspector["Remote Inspector"]
    end
    
    AutoSwitch -->|"controls"| RemoteTree
    StackTrace -->|"affects"| DebuggerPanel["Debugger Panel"]
    MaxNodes -->|"limits"| Inspector
    ProfileNative -->|"enables"| Profiler
    FrameHistory -->|"configures"| Profiler
    MaxFunctions -->|"limits"| Profiler
    TargetFPS -->|"displays"| Profiler
    InspectInterval -->|"throttles"| Inspector
    SceneInterval -->|"throttles"| RemoteTree
```

**Key Debugger Settings**

The debugger settings control runtime debugging behavior and performance:

- **`debugger/max_node_selection`**: Limits how many remote nodes can be selected simultaneously (default varies, typically 8-16). Prevents performance issues when inspecting large node counts.

- **`debugger/profile_native_calls`**: When enabled, includes native C++ engine method calls in profiler results. Adds overhead but provides complete profiling data.

- **`debugger/profiler_frame_history_size`**: Number of frames buffered for profiler graphs (default 3600 = 60 seconds at 60 FPS).

- **`debugger/remote_scene_tree_refresh_interval`**: Controls update frequency for the remote scene tree display. Lower values increase responsiveness but may cause stuttering.

Sources: [doc/classes/EditorSettings.xml:250-279](), [editor/settings/editor_settings.cpp:459]()

### Debugger Message Transmission

Settings are transmitted to running game instances through the `GameViewDebugger::_session_started()` method, which sends a dictionary of relevant settings including selection colors, navigation schemes, and debugger limits.

Sources: [editor/run/game_view_plugin.cpp:62-117]()

## SceneDebugger System

### Architecture and Message Handling

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Editor Side"
        DebuggerNode["EditorDebuggerNode"]
        Session["EditorDebuggerSession"]
        Send["send_message()"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Runtime Side (Game Process)"
        ED["EngineDebugger"]
        SD["SceneDebugger<br/>Singleton"]
        ParseMsg["parse_message()"]
        Handlers["message_handlers<br/>HashMap"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Subsystems"
        LE["LiveEditor<br/>Scene modification"]
        RNS["RuntimeNodeSelect<br/>In-game selection"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Message Types"
        SceneTree["request_scene_tree"]
        InspectObj["inspect_objects"]
        SetProp["set_object_property"]
        LiveEdit["live_* messages"]
        SelectMsg["runtime_node_select_*"]
    end
    
    DebuggerNode -->|"creates"| Session
    Session -->|"calls"| Send
    Send -.->|"network"| ED
    
    ED -->|"routes 'scene' capture"| SD
    SD -->|"dispatches"| ParseMsg
    ParseMsg -->|"looks up"| Handlers
    
    Handlers -->|"delegates to"| LE
    Handlers -->|"delegates to"| RNS
    
    SceneTree -->|"handled by"| Handlers
    InspectObj -->|"handled by"| Handlers
    SetProp -->|"handled by"| Handlers
    LiveEdit -->|"handled by"| LE
    SelectMsg -->|"handled by"| RNS
```

**SceneDebugger Message Protocol**

The `SceneDebugger` class registers with `EngineDebugger` to handle messages with the `"scene"` capture prefix. When messages arrive, `parse_message()` dispatches to registered handlers:

| Message | Handler | Purpose |
|---------|---------|---------|
| `"request_scene_tree"` | `_msg_request_scene_tree()` | Send scene hierarchy to editor |
| `"inspect_objects"` | `_msg_inspect_objects()` | Serialize object properties for inspector |
| `"set_object_property"` | `_msg_set_object_property()` | Modify object property at runtime |
| `"live_set_root"` | `_msg_live_set_root()` | Live editing: set scene root |
| `"runtime_node_select_setup"` | `_msg_runtime_node_select_setup()` | Initialize node selection system |
| `"override_cameras"` | `_msg_override_cameras()` | Enable/disable camera override for debugging |

The message handler map is initialized in `_init_message_handlers()` during `SceneDebugger::initialize()`.

Sources: [scene/debugger/scene_debugger.cpp:65-106](), [scene/debugger/scene_debugger.cpp:524-599](), [scene/debugger/scene_debugger.h:54-96]()

### Live Editing Capabilities

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "LiveEditor Operations"
        NodeOps["Node Operations<br/>create, remove, reparent"]
        PropOps["Property Operations<br/>set properties/resources"]
        CallOps["Method Calls<br/>call functions"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Message Flow"
        EditorSend["Editor sends live_* message"]
        MsgHandler["SceneDebugger routes to LiveEditor"]
        Execute["LiveEditor executes operation"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Examples"
        CreateNode["live_create_node<br/>Add new child node"]
        SetNodeProp["live_node_prop<br/>Modify node property"]
        RemoveNode["live_remove_node<br/>Delete node from scene"]
        ReparentNode["live_reparent_node<br/>Move node in hierarchy"]
    end
    
    EditorSend --> MsgHandler
    MsgHandler --> Execute
    
    NodeOps --> CreateNode
    PropOps --> SetNodeProp
    NodeOps --> RemoveNode
    NodeOps --> ReparentNode
    
    Execute -.->|"modifies"| RunningScene["Running Scene Tree"]
```

**Live Editing Message Handlers**

Live editing allows the editor to modify a running game without restarting. Key operations:

- **Node Creation**: `live_create_node` instantiates a new node and adds it to the scene
- **Node Removal**: `live_remove_node` deletes a node (with optional keep for restore)
- **Property Modification**: `live_node_prop` and `live_res_prop` update properties on nodes/resources
- **Node Reparenting**: `live_reparent_node` moves nodes in the scene hierarchy
- **Method Invocation**: `live_node_call` and `live_res_call` execute methods with arguments

Each operation is executed immediately in the running game process. The `RuntimeNodeSelect` system automatically updates selection display after structural changes.

Sources: [scene/debugger/scene_debugger.cpp:268-381](), [scene/debugger/scene_debugger.h:86-95]()

## RuntimeNodeSelect System

### In-Game Selection Architecture

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "RuntimeNodeSelect Singleton"
        RNS["RuntimeNodeSelect"]
        Settings["Configuration<br/>SelectMode, NodeType, colors"]
        Selection["selected_nodes<br/>Vector<Node*>"]
        Visual["Visual Feedback<br/>CanvasItem overlays"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Selection Modes"
        Click["CLICK_SELECT<br/>Click to select"]
        Hover["HOVER_SELECT<br/>Hover to select"]
        None["NONE<br/>Selection disabled"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Node Types"
        CanvasItem2D["CANVAS_ITEM<br/>2D nodes"]
        Node3DType["NODE_3D<br/>3D nodes"]
        BothTypes["BOTH<br/>2D and 3D"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Rendering"
        Draw2D["_draw_selection_2d()<br/>Box/transform display"]
        Draw3D["_draw_selection_3d()<br/>AABB/transform display"]
        CameraOverride["Camera override for visibility"]
    end
    
    RNS -->|"configured by"| Settings
    RNS -->|"maintains"| Selection
    RNS -->|"renders"| Visual
    
    Settings -->|"mode"| Click
    Settings -->|"mode"| Hover
    Settings -->|"mode"| None
    
    Settings -->|"type"| CanvasItem2D
    Settings -->|"type"| Node3DType
    Settings -->|"type"| BothTypes
    
    Visual -->|"2D rendering"| Draw2D
    Visual -->|"3D rendering"| Draw3D
    Visual -->|"requires"| CameraOverride
```

**RuntimeNodeSelect Configuration**

The `RuntimeNodeSelect` singleton enables in-game node selection for debugging. Configuration is sent via `runtime_node_select_setup` message containing:

```cpp
// From editor/run/game_view_plugin.cpp:68-76
Dictionary settings;
settings["debugger/max_node_selection"] = EDITOR_GET("debugger/max_node_selection");
settings["editors/2d/selection_rectangle_color"] = EDITOR_GET("editors/2d/selection_rectangle_color");
settings["box_selection_fill_color"] = theme->get_color("box_selection_fill_color", "Editor");
```

Selection behavior is controlled by:
- **SelectMode**: `CLICK_SELECT`, `HOVER_SELECT`, or `NONE`
- **NodeType**: `CANVAS_ITEM` (2D), `NODE_3D` (3D), or `BOTH`
- **avoid_locked**: Skip locked nodes during selection
- **prefer_group**: Select parent groups instead of individual nodes

Sources: [scene/debugger/runtime_node_select.h:40-90](), [scene/debugger/runtime_node_select.cpp:1-100]()

### Selection Rendering

The system renders selection feedback using:

- **2D Selection**: Draws bounding boxes and transform gizmos using `CanvasItem` draw commands with colors from editor settings
- **3D Selection**: Renders AABBs and position indicators using immediate mesh geometry
- **Camera Override**: Enables a debug camera controlled from the editor to inspect from different angles

Selection updates occur when the editor sends `inspect_objects` messages or when nodes are modified through live editing.

Sources: [scene/debugger/runtime_node_select.cpp:200-400](), [scene/debugger/scene_debugger.cpp:636-677]()

**3D Navigation Presets**

The 3D editor supports multiple navigation schemes controlled by `editors/3d/navigation/navigation_scheme`:

| Scheme | Orbit | Pan | Zoom | Notes |
|--------|-------|-----|------|-------|
| **Godot** (0) | Middle Mouse | Shift+Middle | Ctrl+Middle | Default scheme |
| **Maya** (1) | Alt+Left | Middle | Alt+Right | Industry standard |
| **Modo** (2) | Alt+Left | Alt+Shift+Left | Ctrl+Alt+Left | Alternative workflow |
| **Tablet/Trackpad** (3) | Alt | Shift | Ctrl | Enables 3-button emulation |
| **Custom** (4) | User-defined | User-defined | User-defined | Manual configuration |

When a preset is selected, `update_navigation_preset()` automatically configures the individual mouse button settings. Changing any button manually sets the scheme to Custom.

Sources: [doc/classes/EditorSettings.xml:457-465](), [editor/settings/editor_settings_dialog.cpp:97-140]()

### 2D Editor Configuration

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "2D Editor Settings"

```

**2D Editor Visual Settings**

The 2D canvas editor uses settings to control visual appearance:

- **Grid Display**: `editors/2d/grid_color` and step/offset values control the background grid
- **Selection Feedback**: `editors/2d/selection_rectangle_color` for selected node outlines, `editors/2d/locked_selection_rectangle_color` for locked nodes
- **Smart Snapping**: `editors/2d/smart_snapping_line_color` renders alignment guides when moving nodes
- **Skeleton Editor**: `bone_color1`, `bone_color2`, `bone_ik_color` colorize bone display

Grid configuration is exposed through the `SnapDialog` accessible from the canvas toolbar.

Sources: [doc/classes/EditorSettings.xml:323-375](), [editor/scene/canvas_item_editor_plugin.cpp:83-235]()

### Settings Persistence and Change Notification

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Change Detection"
        Set["EditorSettings::_set()"]
        Changed["changed_settings.insert()"]
        Signal["emit_signal('settings_changed')"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Listeners"
        SettingsDialog["EditorSettingsDialog"]
        Viewports["Editor Viewports"]
        Debugger["Debugger Systems"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Persistence"
        Timer["Auto-save timer"]
        Save["save() to editor_settings-4.tres"]
        Optimize["optimize_save flag<br/>Only save non-default values"]
    end
    
    Set -->|"marks change"| Changed
    Changed -->|"triggers"| Signal
    Signal -->|"notifies"| SettingsDialog
    Signal -->|"notifies"| Viewports
    Signal -->|"notifies"| Debugger
    
    Changed -->|"starts"| Timer
    Timer -->|"calls"| Save
    Save -->|"respects"| Optimize
```

**Settings Change Propagation**

When a setting is modified through `set_setting()` or the inspector:

1. `_set()` updates the value in `props` and adds the key to `changed_settings`
2. `settings_changed` signal is emitted to notify listeners
3. A timer starts that will trigger auto-save after a brief delay
4. Listeners update their state based on the new setting

Special handling exists for certain settings:
- Changing navigation mouse buttons automatically sets `navigation_scheme` to Custom
- Modifying theme colors sets theme preset to "Custom"
- Language changes trigger `setup_language()` for UI re-translation

Sources: [editor/settings/editor_settings.cpp:73-100](), [editor/settings/editor_settings_dialog.cpp:67-95]()

## Settings Dialog UI

The `EditorSettingsDialog` provides the user interface for browsing and modifying settings:

- **Tabbed Interface**: Separate tabs for General settings, Shortcuts, and other categories
- **Sectioned Inspector**: Settings organized hierarchically by category (interface/, debugger/, editors/, etc.)
- **Search**: Filter settings by name or category
- **Reset to Default**: Revert button uses stored `initial` values
- **Shortcut Editor**: Visual editor for keyboard shortcuts with conflict detection

The dialog uses `EditorSectionedInspector` to display settings organized by their slash-delimited paths (e.g., `debugger/max_node_selection` appears under "Debugger" â†’ "Max Node Selection").

Sources: [editor/settings/editor_settings_dialog.h:50-120](), [editor/settings/editor_settings_dialog.cpp:60-95]()26:T5482,# GUI System

## Purpose and Scope

The GUI System provides the framework for building user interfaces in Godot. It encompasses the base `Control` node class, layout mechanisms, text rendering components, theming, and input event routing. This system handles everything from simple labels to complex text editors.

For information about viewport rendering and canvas drawing, see [Viewport and Rendering Integration](#2.3). For details about input event flow at the scene tree level, see [Input Processing and GUI Events](#5.3). For control-specific layout and theming details, see [Control Nodes and Layout System](#5.1). For text components specifically, see [Text Editing Components](#5.2).

---

## Control Node Hierarchy

The GUI system is built around a hierarchy of `Control` nodes, all inheriting from the base `Control` class. Below is the inheritance structure for the core GUI components:

```mermaid
graph TB
    Object["Object"]
    Node["Node<br/>scene/main/node.h"]
    CanvasItem["CanvasItem<br/>2D Drawing Interface"]
    Control["Control<br/>scene/gui/control.h<br/>Base UI Node"]
    
    Label["Label<br/>scene/gui/label.h<br/>Simple Text Display"]
    LineEdit["LineEdit<br/>scene/gui/line_edit.h<br/>Single-Line Input"]
    TextEdit["TextEdit<br/>scene/gui/text_edit.h<br/>Multi-Line Editor"]
    RichTextLabel["RichTextLabel<br/>scene/gui/rich_text_label.h<br/>Formatted Text"]
    CodeEdit["CodeEdit<br/>scene/gui/code_edit.h<br/>Code Editor"]
    Container["Container<br/>Layout Management"]
    
    Object --> Node
    Node --> CanvasItem
    CanvasItem --> Control
    
    Control --> Label
    Control --> LineEdit
    Control --> TextEdit
    Control --> RichTextLabel
    Control --> Container
    
    TextEdit --> CodeEdit
```

**Sources:** [scene/gui/control.h:53](), [scene/gui/label.h:1](), [scene/gui/line_edit.h:1](), [scene/gui/text_edit.h:40](), [scene/gui/rich_text_label.h:50](), [scene/gui/code_edit.h:1]()

---

## Architecture Overview

```mermaid
graph TB
    SceneTree["SceneTree<br/>scene/main/scene_tree.h<br/>Main Loop Manager"]
    Viewport["Viewport<br/>scene/main/viewport.h<br/>Input & Rendering Root"]
    Window["Window<br/>scene/main/window.h<br/>OS Window"]
    
    Control["Control<br/>GUI Base Class"]
    CanvasItem["CanvasItem<br/>2D Drawing"]
    
    RenderingServer["RenderingServer<br/>Graphics Backend"]
    TextServer["TextServer<br/>Text Shaping"]
    ThemeDB["ThemeDB<br/>Theme Resources"]
    
    InputEvent["InputEvent<br/>Mouse/Keyboard/Touch"]
    
    SceneTree --> Viewport
    Viewport --> Window
    Window --> Control
    
    Control -.inherits.-> CanvasItem
    CanvasItem --> RenderingServer
    
    InputEvent --> Viewport
    Viewport -->|"gui_input()"| Control
    
    Control --> TextServer
    Control --> ThemeDB
```

**Architecture Components:**

The GUI system sits within the scene tree hierarchy, with `Control` nodes as specialized `CanvasItem` nodes. The `Viewport` class manages input routing and determines which `Control` node receives events based on z-order, mouse filters, and focus state.

**Sources:** [scene/main/viewport.h:95](), [scene/gui/control.h:53](), [scene/main/scene_tree.h:1](), [scene/main/window.h:1]()

---

## The Control Base Class

### Class Definition and Core Properties

`Control` is defined in [scene/gui/control.h:53-67]() and inherits from `CanvasItem`. It adds GUI-specific functionality including:

| Property Category | Key Members | Location |
|------------------|-------------|----------|
| **Layout** | `data.anchor[]`, `data.offset[]`, `data.size` | [scene/gui/control.h:1]() |
| **Transform** | `data.rotation`, `data.scale`, `data.pivot_offset` | [scene/gui/control.cpp:89-92]() |
| **Theming** | `theme_icon_override`, `theme_style_override`, `theme_font_override` | [scene/gui/control.h:1]() |
| **Input** | `data.mouse_filter`, `data.key_focus`, `data.default_cursor_shape` | [scene/gui/control.h:1]() |
| **Visibility** | `data.clip_contents`, `data.toplevel` | [scene/gui/control.cpp:1]() |

### Layout System

Controls use an anchor-and-offset system for positioning:

```mermaid
graph LR
    Parent["Parent Control<br/>or Viewport"]
    Anchors["Anchors<br/>data.anchor[SIDE_*]<br/>Relative Positions 0.0-1.0"]
    Offsets["Offsets<br/>data.offset[SIDE_*]<br/>Pixel Adjustments"]
    FinalPos["Final Rect<br/>Position + Size"]
    
    Parent --> Anchors
    Anchors --> Offsets
    Offsets --> FinalPos
```

**Anchor Calculation:**
- Anchors are stored per-side in `data.anchor[SIDE_LEFT/TOP/RIGHT/BOTTOM]` [scene/gui/control.h:1]()
- Range: 0.0 (parent's left/top) to 1.0 (parent's right/bottom)
- Applied in `_size_changed()` [scene/gui/control.cpp:1]()

**Offset Calculation:**
- Offsets are in `data.offset[SIDE_*]` [scene/gui/control.h:1]()
- Added to anchor-based position to get final pixel coordinates
- Supports negative values for right/bottom-anchored controls

**Sources:** [scene/gui/control.h:1](), [scene/gui/control.cpp:1]()

---

## Text Components Architecture

The GUI system includes specialized text display and editing components, all using `TextServer` for text shaping and `TextParagraph` for layout:

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Text Rendering Pipeline"
        TextServer["TextServer<br/>servers/text/text_server.h<br/>Text Shaping & BiDi"]
        TextParagraph["TextParagraph<br/>scene/resources/text_paragraph.h<br/>Line Breaking & Layout"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Display Components"
        Label["Label<br/>scene/gui/label.h<br/>text_buf: TextParagraph"]
        RichTextLabel["RichTextLabel<br/>scene/gui/rich_text_label.h<br/>Item-Based Formatting"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Edit Components"
        LineEdit["LineEdit<br/>scene/gui/line_edit.h<br/>text_rid: RID"]
        TextEdit["TextEdit<br/>scene/gui/text_edit.h<br/>Text::Line::data_buf"]
        CodeEdit["CodeEdit<br/>scene/gui/code_edit.h<br/>Extends TextEdit"]
    end
    
    TextServer --> TextParagraph
    
    TextParagraph --> Label
    TextParagraph --> RichTextLabel
    TextParagraph --> TextEdit
    
    TextServer --> LineEdit
    TextEdit --> CodeEdit
```

### Label Component

`Label` [scene/gui/label.h:1]() is the simplest text display control:
- Single `TextParagraph` instance: `text_buf` [scene/gui/label.cpp:1]()
- Supports word wrapping via `autowrap_mode`
- Uses theme font/font_size from `theme_cache`
- Rendering in `_notification(NOTIFICATION_DRAW)` [scene/gui/label.cpp:1]()

### TextEdit Component

`TextEdit` [scene/gui/text_edit.h:40]() is a complex multiline editor with the following architecture:

**Internal Text Storage:**
```mermaid
graph TB
    TextEdit["TextEdit"]
    Text["Text Class<br/>text_edit.h:136<br/>Manages Lines"]
    Line["Line Struct<br/>text_edit.h:149<br/>Per-Line Data"]
    TextParagraph_Line["data_buf: TextParagraph<br/>Shaped Text"]
    Gutters["gutters: Vector&lt;Gutter&gt;<br/>Line Metadata"]
    
    TextEdit --> Text
    Text -->|"Vector&lt;Line&gt; text"| Line
    Line --> TextParagraph_Line
    Line --> Gutters
```

Key mechanisms in `TextEdit`:
- **Line Management**: `Text` class [scene/gui/text_edit.h:136-262]() stores a `Vector<Line>` [scene/gui/text_edit.h:176]()
- **Text Shaping**: Each line has `data_buf.instantiate()` creating a `TextParagraph` [scene/gui/text_edit.h:167-169]()
- **Invalidation**: `invalidate_cache(int p_line)` reshapes lines when text changes [scene/gui/text_edit.cpp:272-398]()
- **Caret System**: Multiple carets supported via `carets` vector [scene/gui/text_edit.cpp:1]()
- **Gutters**: Configurable left margin with icons/text/custom drawing [scene/gui/text_edit.h:125-134]()

### RichTextLabel Component

`RichTextLabel` [scene/gui/rich_text_label.h:50]() uses an item-based approach for formatted text:

**Item System:**
```mermaid
graph TB
    RichTextLabel["RichTextLabel"]
    ItemFrame["ItemFrame<br/>Root Container"]
    ItemText["ItemText<br/>Plain Text Runs"]
    ItemImage["ItemImage<br/>Inline Images"]
    ItemFont["ItemFont<br/>Font Changes"]
    ItemColor["ItemColor<br/>Color Changes"]
    ItemTable["ItemTable<br/>Table Layout"]
    
    RichTextLabel -->|"main: ItemFrame*"| ItemFrame
    ItemFrame -->|"subitems"| ItemText
    ItemFrame -->|"subitems"| ItemImage
    ItemFrame -->|"subitems"| ItemFont
    ItemFrame -->|"subitems"| ItemColor
    ItemFrame -->|"subitems"| ItemTable
```

Items defined in [scene/gui/rich_text_label.h:77-230]():
- **ItemFrame**: Container with lines, each containing `text_buf: TextParagraph` [scene/gui/rich_text_label.h:1]()
- **ItemText**: Stores text content [scene/gui/rich_text_label.h:1]()
- **ItemImage**: Inline images with sizing [scene/gui/rich_text_label.h:1]()
- **ItemFont/ItemColor/ItemFontSize**: Formatting changes [scene/gui/rich_text_label.h:1]()

Text layout occurs in `_shape_line()` [scene/gui/rich_text_label.cpp:647-1000]() which builds the `TextParagraph` by iterating items.

### LineEdit Component

`LineEdit` [scene/gui/line_edit.h:1]() provides single-line text input:
- Direct `RID text_rid` from `TextServer` [scene/gui/line_edit.h:1]()
- Caret positioning via `caret_column` [scene/gui/line_edit.h:1]()
- Selection tracking in `selection` struct [scene/gui/line_edit.h:1]()
- IME support via `ime_text` and `ime_selection` [scene/gui/line_edit.cpp:149-183]()

### CodeEdit Component

`CodeEdit` [scene/gui/code_edit.h:1]() extends `TextEdit` with programming features:
- Code folding
- Auto-indentation  
- Syntax highlighting integration
- Code completion
- Breakpoint management

**Sources:** [scene/gui/label.h:1](), [scene/gui/text_edit.h:40](), [scene/gui/rich_text_label.h:50](), [scene/gui/line_edit.h:1](), [scene/gui/code_edit.h:1]()
