## Purpose and Scope

The Scripting System provides the infrastructure for attaching script code to scene nodes and executing that code at runtime. This document covers the abstract `ScriptLanguage` interface, script resources, script instances, and how scripts integrate with the node hierarchy. The two primary language implementationsâ€”GDScript and C#â€”are introduced here, with detailed pipeline documentation available in their respective pages.

For GDScript's complete compilation pipeline (parsing, analysis, compilation, and execution), see [GDScript Architecture](#6.1). For details on how scripts attach to nodes and their lifecycle methods, see [Script Integration and Lifecycle](#6.2).

## Architecture Overview

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Script Language Interface"
        SL["ScriptLanguage<br/>(Abstract Base)"]
        GDSLang["GDScriptLanguage"]
        CSLang["CSharpLanguage"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Script Resources"
        Script["Script<br/>(Base Class)"]
        GDScript["GDScript"]
        CSharpScript["CSharpScript"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Script Instances"
        ScriptInst["ScriptInstance<br/>(Interface)"]
        GDSInst["GDScriptInstance"]
        CSInst["CSharpInstance"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Scene Integration"
        Node["Node"]
        NodeScript["node.script property"]
        LifecycleMethods["_ready(), _process(), etc."]
    end
    
    SL -.implements.-> GDSLang
    SL -.implements.-> CSLang
    
    Script -.extends.-> GDScript
    Script -.extends.-> CSharpScript
    
    ScriptInst -.implements.-> GDSInst
    ScriptInst -.implements.-> CSInst
    
    GDSLang -->|"creates"| GDScript
    CSLang -->|"creates"| CSharpScript
    
    GDScript -->|"instantiates"| GDSInst
    CSharpScript -->|"instantiates"| CSInst
    
    Node -->|"has"| NodeScript
    NodeScript -->|"references"| Script
    Script -->|"creates"| ScriptInst
    ScriptInst -->|"implements"| LifecycleMethods
```

**Architecture Diagram: Scripting System Components**

The scripting system uses a three-layer architecture: **ScriptLanguage** manages the language runtime, **Script** resources contain the source code and compiled data, and **ScriptInstance** objects attach to nodes and execute script methods.

Sources: [core/object/script_language.h:1-682](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:1-355](), [modules/mono/csharp_script.h:1-313]()

## ScriptLanguage Base Interface

The `ScriptLanguage` class defines the abstract interface that all scripting language implementations must provide. The engine queries script languages through this interface without knowing implementation details.

### Core Language Capabilities

| Method | Purpose |
|--------|---------|
| `get_name()` | Returns language name (e.g., "GDScript", "C#") |
| `get_type()` | Returns script resource type name |
| `get_extension()` | Returns file extension (e.g., "gd", "cs") |
| `get_recognized_extensions()` | Returns list of valid file extensions |
| `make_template()` | Creates a new script from a template string |
| `validate()` | Parses and validates script source code |

**Sources:** [core/object/script_language.h:235-332]()

### Script Loading and Management

```mermaid
graph LR
    FileSystem["File System<br/>.gd or .cs file"] --> ResourceLoader["ResourceLoader"]
    ResourceLoader --> ScriptLanguage["ScriptLanguage::create_script()"]
    ScriptLanguage --> Script["Script Resource"]
    Script --> Parse["Language-specific<br/>parsing/compilation"]
    Parse --> Ready["Script ready<br/>for instantiation"]
```

**Script Loading Flow**

Languages implement `create_script()` to instantiate a `Script` resource from a file path. The script resource manages source code, compiled bytecode (for GDScript), or type metadata (for C#).

**Sources:** [core/object/script_language.cpp:133-179](), [core/object/script_language.h:235-332]()

### Global Script State Management

Each `ScriptLanguage` maintains global state including:

- **Script list**: All loaded scripts for the language ([modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:189]())
- **Global namespace**: Autoloads, singletons, and global script classes
- **Debugging state**: Stack frames, breakpoints, profiling data

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:1-2500](), [modules/mono/csharp_script.cpp:1-1000]()

## Script Resource Class

The `Script` class (subclassed by `GDScript` and `CSharpScript`) represents compiled script code and provides the interface for instantiation.

### Key Script Properties

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class Script {
        +String source
        +String path
        +can_instantiate() bool
        +instance_create(Object) ScriptInstance
        +get_base_script() Ref~Script~
        +get_instance_base_type() StringName
        +has_method(StringName) bool
        +get_method_info(StringName) MethodInfo
    }
    
    class GDScript {
        +bool valid
        +bool tool
        +Ref~GDScriptNativeClass~ native
        +Ref~GDScript~ base
        +HashMap member_functions
        +HashMap member_indices
        +GDScriptFunction* initializer
        +Vector~uint8_t~ binary_tokens
    }
    
    class CSharpScript {
        +TypeInfo type_info
        +bool valid
        +Ref~CSharpScript~ base_script
        +Vector~EventSignalInfo~ event_signals
        +Vector~CSharpMethodInfo~ methods
    }
    
    Script <|-- GDScript
    Script <|-- CSharpScript
```

**Script Class Hierarchy**

**Sources:** [core/object/script_language.h:62-231](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:60-282](), [modules/mono/csharp_script.h:58-205]()

### GDScript Storage

GDScript stores both source and compiled bytecode:

- **source**: The original `.gd` file text ([modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:181]())
- **binary_tokens**: Compiled bytecode for the tokenizer ([modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:182]())
- **member_functions**: Hash map of function name to `GDScriptFunction*` ([modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:107]())
- **member_indices**: Variable names mapped to indices and metadata ([modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:99]())
- **initializer**: Direct pointer to the constructor function ([modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:168]())

GDScript maintains a hierarchy through the `base` pointer to parent scripts and `native` pointer to the base engine class.

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:60-355](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:254-440]()

### CSharpScript Storage

CSharpScript stores type metadata extracted from the compiled .NET assembly:

- **type_info**: C# class name, native base class, tool/global flags ([modules/mono/csharp_script.h:65-126]())
- **event_signals**: C# events exposed as Godot signals ([modules/mono/csharp_script.h:179-182]())
- **methods**: Cached method metadata for editor inspection ([modules/mono/csharp_script.h:184-187]())
- **rpc_config**: Network RPC configuration dictionary ([modules/mono/csharp_script.h:177]())

C# scripts don't store bytecode since the CLR manages compiled assemblies.

**Sources:** [modules/mono/csharp_script.h:58-205](), [modules/mono/csharp_script.cpp:254-780]()

## ScriptInstance Interface

The `ScriptInstance` interface connects a script to a specific object (usually a `Node`). Each object can have one script instance attached via `Object::set_script_instance()`.

### Instance Lifecycle

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Node
    participant Script
    participant ScriptInstance
    participant Language
    
    Node->>Script: instance_create(this)
    Script->>ScriptInstance: new GDScriptInstance()
    ScriptInstance->>ScriptInstance: Initialize members
    Script->>Language: Register instance
    Script->>ScriptInstance: Call @implicit_new()
    Script->>ScriptInstance: Call _init() constructor
    ScriptInstance-->>Node: Return instance
    Node->>Node: set_script_instance()
    
    Note over Node,ScriptInstance: Node now has script attached
    
    Node->>ScriptInstance: _ready()
    Node->>ScriptInstance: _process(delta)
    Node->>ScriptInstance: custom_method()
```

**Script Instance Creation and Lifecycle**

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:153-207](), [modules/mono/csharp_script.cpp:1200-1350]()

### ScriptInstance Method Dispatch

The `ScriptInstance` interface provides several method invocation patterns:

| Method | Purpose |
|--------|---------|
| `call()` / `callp()` | Invoke a script method by name |
| `notification()` | Handle Godot notification messages |
| `get()` / `set()` | Access script properties |
| `get_property_list()` | Enumerate script properties (for inspector) |
| `get_method_list()` | Enumerate script methods |

When the engine calls a method on a node with a script, it first checks if `ScriptInstance` handles the method. If not, it falls back to the node's native implementation.

**Sources:** [core/object/script_language.h:62-135](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:870-1100]()

## GDScript Implementation Overview

GDScript uses a complete compilation pipeline from source text to bytecode execution. The key classes are:

### GDScript Pipeline Components

| Component | Class | Purpose |
|-----------|-------|---------|
| **Tokenizer** | `GDScriptTokenizerText` | Lexical analysis, converts source to tokens |
| **Parser** | `GDScriptParser` | Syntax analysis, builds Abstract Syntax Tree |
| **Analyzer** | `GDScriptAnalyzer` | Semantic analysis, type checking, name resolution |
| **Compiler** | `GDScriptCompiler` | Code generation, converts AST to bytecode |
| **Function** | `GDScriptFunction` | Bytecode container with metadata |
| **VM** | `GDScriptFunction::call()` | Bytecode interpreter |
| **Cache** | `GDScriptCache` | Manages parser/script references |

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_parser.cpp:429-569](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_analyzer.cpp:1-5500](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_compiler.cpp:1-3000]()

### GDScript Compilation Flow

```mermaid
graph TB
    Source["Source Code<br/>.gd file"] --> Tokenizer["GDScriptTokenizerText"]
    Tokenizer --> Tokens["Token Stream"]
    Tokens --> Parser["GDScriptParser::parse()"]
    Parser --> AST["Abstract Syntax Tree<br/>ClassNode, FunctionNode, etc."]
    
    AST --> Analyzer["GDScriptAnalyzer"]
    Analyzer --> ResolveInheritance["resolve_inheritance()"]
    ResolveInheritance --> ResolveInterface["resolve_interface()"]
    ResolveInterface --> ResolveBody["resolve_body()"]
    ResolveBody --> TypedAST["Fully Analyzed AST<br/>with DataTypes"]
    
    TypedAST --> Compiler["GDScriptCompiler"]
    Compiler --> BytecodeGen["GDScriptByteCodeGenerator"]
    BytecodeGen --> Functions["GDScriptFunction objects<br/>with bytecode"]
    
    Functions --> GDScript["GDScript resource"]
    GDScript --> Ready["Ready for instantiation"]
```

**GDScript Compilation Pipeline**

The pipeline progresses through distinct phases, with each phase only running when needed (lazy evaluation). Errors at any phase prevent subsequent phases from executing.

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_parser.cpp:429-528](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_analyzer.cpp:346-632](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_compiler.cpp:1-3000]()

### GDScriptInstance Execution

`GDScriptInstance` stores per-instance data and delegates method calls to `GDScriptFunction::call()`:

- **members**: Array of member variable values ([modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:157]())
- **script**: Reference to the `GDScript` resource
- **owner**: Pointer to the node/object
- **owner_id**: Cached object ID for validation

When a method is called, `GDScriptInstance` looks up the function in the script's `member_functions` map and invokes the bytecode VM.

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:870-1100](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_vm.cpp:1-3000]()

## C# Scripting Implementation

C# scripts integrate with the Mono/.NET runtime rather than using a custom VM. The key difference is that C# compilation happens externally (via MSBuild or similar), and Godot loads the resulting assemblies.

### CSharpScript Loading Process

```mermaid
graph TB
    SourceFile[".cs Source File"] --> Build["External Build<br/>MSBuild/dotnet"]
    Build --> Assembly[".dll Assembly"]
    Assembly --> GDMono["GDMono Runtime"]
    GDMono --> LoadAssembly["Load Assembly"]
    LoadAssembly --> Reflection["Type Reflection"]
    Reflection --> TypeInfo["Extract TypeInfo:<br/>class name, methods,<br/>properties, signals"]
    TypeInfo --> CSharpScript["CSharpScript Resource"]
    CSharpScript --> Ready["Ready for instantiation"]
```

**C# Script Loading and Type Extraction**

Unlike GDScript which compiles on load, C# scripts must be pre-compiled. Godot uses reflection to extract metadata from the compiled types.

**Sources:** [modules/mono/csharp_script.cpp:76-134](), [modules/mono/csharp_script.h:65-126]()

### CSharpInstance and Managed Objects

`CSharpInstance` wraps a managed C# object handle:

- **gchandle**: A `MonoGCHandleData` reference to the managed object ([modules/mono/csharp_script.h:217-242]())
- **script**: The `CSharpScript` that created this instance
- **owner**: The Godot object (Node) this script is attached to

Method calls are marshaled from native Godot code to the managed C# object through the Mono interop layer.

**Sources:** [modules/mono/csharp_script.cpp:1200-1500](), [modules/mono/csharp_script.h:217-313]()

### Managed Callbacks and Interop

The C# integration uses managed callbacks for common operations:

- `ScriptManagerBridge_GetGlobalClassName`: Extract global class metadata
- `ScriptManagerBridge_FrameCallback`: Per-frame processing
- `GCHandleBridge_*`: GC handle management
- `DelegateUtils_*`: Callable marshaling

These callbacks are set up during Mono initialization and allow the C# runtime to call back into the engine.

**Sources:** [modules/mono/csharp_script.cpp:535-539](), [modules/mono/mono_gd/gd_mono_cache.h]()

## Script Registration and Language Server

The `ScriptServer` singleton manages all registered script languages:

```mermaid
graph TB
    ScriptServer["ScriptServer<br/>(Singleton)"]
    ScriptServer --> GDSLang["GDScriptLanguage"]
    ScriptServer --> CSLang["CSharpLanguage"]
    ScriptServer --> OtherLangs["Other Languages<br/>(via GDExtension)"]
    
    ResourceLoader["ResourceLoader"] --> ScriptServer
    ScriptServer --> CorrectLang["Route to correct<br/>language by extension"]
```

**ScriptServer Language Registration**

Each language registers itself with `ScriptServer` during initialization. When loading a script resource, the server determines which language to use based on file extension.

**Sources:** [core/object/script_language.cpp:133-230](), [core/object/script_language.h:428-521]()

## Tool Scripts and Editor Execution

Scripts marked with the `@tool` annotation (GDScript) or `[Tool]` attribute (C#) execute inside the editor:

- **tool**: Boolean flag on `GDScript` and `CSharpScript` ([modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:62](), [modules/mono/csharp_script.h:84]())
- **Execution context**: Tool scripts run during scene editing, not just game runtime
- **Editor safety**: Tool scripts must check `Engine.is_editor_hint()` to avoid unwanted side effects

Tool scripts enable editor plugins, custom inspectors, and procedural generation workflows.

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:254-260](), [modules/mono/csharp_script.cpp:254-260]()

## Script Reloading and Hot Reload

The engine supports reloading scripts at runtime for rapid iteration:

### GDScript Reloading

GDScript implements complete hot reload:

1. Parse and compile the new version
2. Migrate instance data from old to new script
3. Update all function pointers
4. Restore member values where possible

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:1800-2100]()

### C# Assembly Reloading

C# hot reload is more complex due to .NET's assembly loading model:

1. Detect assembly changes via file watcher
2. Serialize managed object state
3. Unload collectible assembly (if supported)
4. Load new assembly version
5. Deserialize and restore object state

C# hot reload is editor-only and requires collectible assemblies (not available in export builds).

**Sources:** [modules/mono/csharp_script.cpp:563-697](), [modules/mono/csharp_script.h:154-168]()

## Script Validation and Error Reporting

Languages implement `validate()` to check script syntax and semantics without full compilation:

```mermaid
graph LR
    Source["Script Source"] --> Validate["ScriptLanguage::validate()"]
    Validate --> Parse["Parse/Analyze"]
    Parse --> Errors["List errors"]
    Parse --> Warnings["List warnings"]
    Parse --> SafeLines["List safe lines<br/>(for debugger)"]
    Errors --> Report["Report to editor"]
    Warnings --> Report
    SafeLines --> Debugger["Script Debugger"]
```

**Script Validation Flow**

Validation runs when the script is edited and provides immediate feedback without executing code.

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_editor.cpp:146-215](), [modules/mono/csharp_script.cpp]()

## Debugging and Stack Traces

Script languages provide debugging support through:

- `debug_get_stack_level_count()`: Number of stack frames
- `debug_get_stack_level_line()`: Line number for a frame
- `debug_get_stack_level_function()`: Function name for a frame
- `debug_get_stack_level_locals()`: Local variables in a frame
- `debug_get_stack_level_members()`: Instance members in a frame

For GDScript, the VM maintains a call stack in thread-local storage during execution. C# uses .NET's `StackTrace` API.

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_editor.cpp:293-462](), [modules/mono/csharp_script.cpp:451-513]()

## Performance Considerations

### GDScript Optimization

- **Bytecode compilation**: Source is compiled once and cached as bytecode
- **Type specialization**: Type hints enable optimized bytecode instructions
- **Function pointers**: Updatable function pointers allow hot reload without performance loss
- **Member caching**: Member indices are cached for O(1) access

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_compiler.cpp:1-3000](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_vm.cpp:1-3000]()

### C# Performance

- **JIT compilation**: .NET JIT produces native machine code
- **Interop overhead**: Marshaling between managed/native has cost
- **GC pressure**: Frequent allocations can trigger garbage collection
- **AOT compilation**: Ahead-of-time compilation for export targets

**Sources:** [modules/mono/csharp_script.cpp:1-2500]()

## Extension via GDExtension

Third-party languages can integrate using the `ScriptLanguageExtension` class, which provides virtual methods for all `ScriptLanguage` operations. Languages like Lua, Python, and others use this system.

**Sources:** [core/object/script_language_extension.h:1-700]()

This document provides an overview of the Scripting System architecture. For detailed information on GDScript's parsing and compilation pipeline, see [GDScript Architecture](#6.1). For script lifecycle integration with nodes and method invocation, see [Script Integration and Lifecycle](#6.2).2b:T60a8,# GDScript Architecture

This document describes the complete GDScript compilation and execution pipeline, including parsing, semantic analysis, bytecode generation, and virtual machine execution. For information about how scripts attach to nodes and their lifecycle methods, see [Script Integration and Lifecycle](#6.2).

## Overview

GDScript is Godot's built-in scripting language, implementing a complete compilation pipeline from source code to bytecode execution. The architecture consists of four major stages operating in sequence:

1. **Tokenization** - Lexical analysis of source code
2. **Parsing** - Generation of Abstract Syntax Tree (AST)
3. **Analysis** - Type checking and semantic validation
4. **Compilation** - Bytecode generation
5. **Execution** - Virtual machine interpretation

The `GDScriptCache` manages dependencies between scripts and ensures efficient reuse of parsed and analyzed results.

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_parser.cpp:1-870](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_analyzer.cpp:1-632](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_compiler.cpp:1-208]()

## Compilation Pipeline

```mermaid
graph TB
    Source["Source Code<br/>(String)"]
    Token["GDScriptTokenizerText"]
    Parser["GDScriptParser"]
    AST["AST<br/>(ClassNode tree)"]
    Analyzer["GDScriptAnalyzer"]
    AnalyzedAST["Analyzed AST<br/>(with DataTypes)"]
    Compiler["GDScriptCompiler"]
    Bytecode["GDScriptFunction<br/>(bytecode)"]
    VM["GDScript VM"]
    
    Source --> Token
    Token --> Parser
    Parser --> AST
    AST --> Analyzer
    Analyzer --> AnalyzedAST
    AnalyzedAST --> Compiler
    Compiler --> Bytecode
    Bytecode --> VM
    
    Cache["GDScriptCache"]
    ParserRef["GDScriptParserRef<br/>(status tracking)"]
    
    Cache -.manages.-> ParserRef
    ParserRef -.owns.-> Parser
    ParserRef -.owns.-> Analyzer
```

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_parser.cpp:429-528](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_cache.cpp:41-112](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_compiler.cpp:1-208]()

## Tokenization

The `GDScriptTokenizerText` class performs lexical analysis, converting source code into a stream of tokens.

### Token Types

| Category | Examples | Purpose |
|----------|----------|---------|
| Keywords | `func`, `var`, `class`, `extends` | Language constructs |
| Operators | `+`, `-`, `==`, `and`, `or` | Expressions and logic |
| Literals | Numbers, strings, `true`, `false` | Constant values |
| Identifiers | Variable/function names | References |
| Special | `@annotation`, `$NodePath` | GDScript-specific |
| Structural | Newlines, indentation | Block structure |

The tokenizer handles Python-like indentation through `INDENT` and `DEDENT` tokens, tracking indentation levels to generate proper block structure.

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_tokenizer.cpp:44-159](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_tokenizer.h:1-196]()

## Parser: AST Generation

The `GDScriptParser` class converts the token stream into an Abstract Syntax Tree (AST), representing the program structure.

### Parser Architecture

```mermaid
graph TB
    Parser["GDScriptParser"]
    Tokenizer["GDScriptTokenizer"]
    
    Parser -->|scan| Tokenizer
    Parser -->|produces| ClassNode
    
    ClassNode["ClassNode<br/>(head)"]
    Members["members[]"]
    
    ClassNode --> Members
    
    Members --> FunctionNode
    Members --> VariableNode
    Members --> SignalNode
    Members --> EnumNode
    Members --> ConstantNode
    Members --> InnerClass["ClassNode<br/>(nested)"]
    
    FunctionNode["FunctionNode"]
    FunctionNode --> Parameters["ParameterNode[]"]
    FunctionNode --> Body["SuiteNode<br/>(function body)"]
    
    Body --> Statements["Statement nodes:<br/>IfNode, ForNode,<br/>WhileNode, etc."]
    Body --> Expressions["Expression nodes:<br/>CallNode, BinaryOpNode,<br/>IdentifierNode, etc."]
```

### Node Hierarchy

All AST nodes inherit from `GDScriptParser::Node` and are categorized:

**Statement Nodes:**
- `IfNode`, `WhileNode`, `ForNode` - Control flow
- `MatchNode`, `MatchBranchNode` - Pattern matching
- `AssignmentNode`, `ReturnNode`, `BreakNode`, `ContinueNode` - Flow control
- `AssertNode`, `BreakpointNode` - Debugging

**Expression Nodes:**
- `CallNode`, `SubscriptNode`, `GetNodeNode` - Operations
- `BinaryOpNode`, `UnaryOpNode`, `TernaryOpNode` - Operators
- `LiteralNode`, `IdentifierNode`, `SelfNode` - Values
- `ArrayNode`, `DictionaryNode` - Collections
- `LambdaNode`, `AwaitNode`, `CastNode` - Advanced features

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_parser.h:54-358](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_parser.cpp:699-870]()

### Parsing Process

The parser operates in a single forward pass, using recursive descent parsing:

1. **`parse_program()`** - Entry point, parses class-level structure
2. **`parse_class_body()`** - Parses class members (functions, variables, etc.)
3. **`parse_statement()`** - Parses individual statements
4. **`parse_expression()`** - Parses expressions with operator precedence

The parser tracks parsing state through:
- `current` and `previous` tokens
- `multiline_stack` for handling multi-line expressions
- `annotation_stack` for pending annotations
- Completion context for IDE integration

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_parser.cpp:699-869](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_parser.cpp:571-697]()

## Analyzer: Type Checking and Semantic Analysis

The `GDScriptAnalyzer` performs semantic analysis on the AST in multiple phases.

### Analysis Phases

```mermaid
graph LR
    AST["Parsed AST"]
    Phase1["Phase 1:<br/>Resolve Inheritance"]
    Phase2["Phase 2:<br/>Resolve Interface"]
    Phase3["Phase 3:<br/>Resolve Body"]
    Complete["Fully Analyzed AST"]
    
    AST --> Phase1
    Phase1 --> Phase2
    Phase2 --> Phase3
    Phase3 --> Complete
    
    Phase1 -.->|"resolves base_type"| ClassNode
    Phase2 -.->|"resolves member types"| Members
    Phase3 -.->|"validates expressions"| Expressions
```

### GDScriptParser::DataType

Each AST node carries a `DataType` describing its type information:

```mermaid
graph TB
    DataType["GDScriptParser::DataType"]
    
    DataType --> Kind["kind enum:<br/>BUILTIN, NATIVE, SCRIPT,<br/>CLASS, ENUM, VARIANT"]
    DataType --> TypeSource["type_source enum:<br/>UNDETECTED, INFERRED,<br/>ANNOTATED_EXPLICIT,<br/>ANNOTATED_INFERRED"]
    DataType --> Properties["Properties:<br/>builtin_type, native_type,<br/>script_type, class_type,<br/>enum_type, enum_values"]
    DataType --> Container["container_element_types[]<br/>(for Array, Dictionary)"]
    DataType --> Flags["Flags:<br/>is_constant, is_read_only,<br/>is_meta_type, is_coroutine"]
```

**Type Kind Categories:**

| Kind | Description | Example |
|------|-------------|---------|
| `BUILTIN` | Built-in Variant types | `int`, `String`, `Array` |
| `NATIVE` | Native engine classes | `Node`, `Resource` |
| `SCRIPT` | Non-GDScript scripts | C# scripts |
| `CLASS` | GDScript classes | User classes |
| `ENUM` | Enumeration types | `Error`, custom enums |
| `VARIANT` | Untyped/dynamic | Default when no annotation |

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_parser.h:101-259](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_analyzer.cpp:54-222]()

### Analysis Process

#### Phase 1: Inheritance Resolution

Resolves `extends` declarations and establishes the class hierarchy:

1. Parses the extends path or class name
2. Loads and analyzes base scripts via `GDScriptCache`
3. Sets `base_type` on the `ClassNode`
4. Validates against cyclic inheritance

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_analyzer.cpp:346-632]()

#### Phase 2: Interface Resolution

Resolves member signatures without analyzing bodies:

1. Resolves variable types from annotations or initializers
2. Resolves function parameter and return types
3. Resolves signal signatures
4. Checks for member name conflicts
5. Builds member indices for the class

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_analyzer.cpp:634-1500]()

#### Phase 3: Body Resolution

Validates all expression nodes and statement logic:

1. Type-checks all expressions
2. Validates assignments and type conversions
3. Resolves identifier references (local, member, global)
4. Checks control flow validity
5. Validates function calls and argument types
6. Performs constant folding when possible

The analyzer reduces constant expressions to their values and stores them in `ExpressionNode::reduced_value`.

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_analyzer.cpp:1502-4000]()

### Type Checking

The analyzer uses these key functions for type validation:

- `resolve_datatype()` - Converts type annotations to `DataType`
- `reduce_identifier()` - Resolves identifier references
- `reduce_expression()` - Type-checks and potentially reduces expressions
- `is_type_compatible()` - Checks if one type can be assigned to another
- `check_type_compatibility()` - Validates type compatibility with error reporting

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_analyzer.cpp:654-850](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_analyzer.cpp:2500-3000]()

## Compiler: Bytecode Generation

The `GDScriptCompiler` translates the analyzed AST into bytecode executed by the GDScript VM.

### Compilation Architecture

```mermaid
graph TB
    Compiler["GDScriptCompiler"]
    CodeGen["GDScriptByteCodeGenerator"]
    Function["GDScriptFunction"]
    
    Compiler -->|uses| CodeGen
    CodeGen -->|generates| Function
    
    Function --> Instructions["instructions[]<br/>(bytecode)"]
    Function --> Constants["constants[]"]
    Function --> Members["member_indices"]
    Function --> Locals["stack_size"]
    
    AST["Analyzed AST"]
    AST -->|input| Compiler
    
    CodeGen --> Addresses["Address Management:<br/>STACK, CONSTANT,<br/>MEMBER, CLASS"]
    CodeGen --> Labels["Jump Labels"]
    CodeGen --> Fixups["Fixup Lists<br/>(for jumps)"]
```

### GDScriptFunction Structure

A compiled `GDScriptFunction` contains:

| Component | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `instructions` | Bytecode instruction stream |
| `constants` | Constant value pool |
| `member_indices` | Class member lookup |
| `argument_types` | Function parameter types |
| `argument_names` | Parameter names |
| `default_arguments` | Default value positions |
| `stack_size` | Maximum stack depth needed |
| `_code_size` | Bytecode size in bytes |
| `_call_size` | Call stack frame size |

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_function.h:98-312](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_function.cpp:1-117]()

### Bytecode Generation Process

The compiler traverses the AST and emits bytecode:

1. **`_compile_class()`** - Compiles a class and its members
2. **`_compile_function()`** - Compiles a function body
3. **`_parse_expression()`** - Generates code for expressions
4. **`_parse_block()`** - Generates code for statement blocks

The `GDScriptByteCodeGenerator` manages:
- Address allocation (stack slots, constants, members)
- Temporary variable tracking
- Jump label resolution
- Instruction emission

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_compiler.cpp:255-2500](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_byte_codegen.cpp:1-2000]()

### Instruction Set

The VM uses a stack-based instruction set with opcodes like:

**Stack Operations:**
- `OPCODE_PUSH_CONSTANT`, `OPCODE_ASSIGN` - Data movement
- `OPCODE_GET_MEMBER`, `OPCODE_SET_MEMBER` - Member access

**Operators:**
- `OPCODE_OPERATOR` - Binary/unary operations
- `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST` - Type checking (`is` operator)

**Control Flow:**
- `OPCODE_JUMP`, `OPCODE_JUMP_IF`, `OPCODE_JUMP_IF_NOT` - Branching
- `OPCODE_RETURN` - Function return

**Calls:**
- `OPCODE_CALL`, `OPCODE_CALL_SELF` - Function calls
- `OPCODE_CALL_BUILTIN`, `OPCODE_CALL_UTILITY` - Built-in functions

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_function.h:34-96]()

### Address Types

The code generator uses different address types for operands:

```mermaid
graph LR
    Address["GDScriptCodeGenerator::Address"]
    
    Address --> NIL["NIL<br/>(no address)"]
    Address --> SELF["SELF<br/>(instance)"]
    Address --> CLASS["CLASS<br/>(script class)"]
    Address --> MEMBER["MEMBER<br/>(instance variable)"]
    Address --> CONSTANT["CONSTANT<br/>(constant pool)"]
    Address --> STACK["STACK<br/>(local/temp)"]
    
    STACK -.->|"includes"| Locals["Local variables"]
    STACK -.->|"includes"| Temps["Temporary results"]
```

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_byte_codegen.h:41-120]()

## Virtual Machine Execution

The GDScript VM executes bytecode through `GDScriptFunction::call()`.

### Execution Model

```mermaid
graph TB
    Call["GDScriptFunction::call()"]
    Stack["Variant* stack"]
    IP["int* ip<br/>(instruction pointer)"]
    
    Call --> Stack
    Call --> IP
    
    Stack --> Locals["Local variables"]
    Stack --> Temps["Temporary values"]
    Stack --> Return["Return value"]
    
    IP --> Decode["Decode instruction"]
    Decode --> Execute["Execute opcode"]
    Execute --> Advance["Advance IP"]
    Advance --> Check{More<br/>instructions?}
    Check -->|Yes| Decode
    Check -->|No| Return
    
    Execute -.->|"reads/writes"| Stack
```

The VM maintains:
- **Call stack** - Function activation records
- **Value stack** - Local variables and temporaries
- **Instruction pointer** - Current bytecode position

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_vm.cpp:1-5000]()

### Instruction Execution

Each instruction is executed in a giant switch statement:

```
switch (opcode) {
    case OPCODE_OPERATOR:
        // Execute operator on stack values
        break;
    case OPCODE_CALL:
        // Resolve and call function
        break;
    // ... hundreds of cases
}
```

The VM handles:
- **Type validation** - Runtime type checking for typed variables
- **Container typing** - Enforcing Array and Dictionary element types
- **Error handling** - Call errors, type mismatches, null dereferencing
- **Profiling** - Performance tracking (debug builds)

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_vm.cpp:155-5000]()

### Call Stack Management

Function calls are managed through `GDScriptLanguage::CallLevel`:

| Field | Purpose |
|-------|---------|
| `function` | Current `GDScriptFunction*` |
| `instance` | Current `GDScriptInstance*` |
| `stack` | Local variable stack |
| `line` | Current source line (debugging) |

The language maintains a global call stack accessible for debugging and error reporting.

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:457-520]()

## Caching and Dependency Management

`GDScriptCache` manages script loading, parsing, and analysis to avoid redundant work.

### Cache Architecture

```mermaid
graph TB
    Cache["GDScriptCache<br/>(static methods)"]
    
    Cache --> ParserCache["parser_map<br/>HashMap&lt;String, GDScriptParserRef&gt;"]
    Cache --> ShallowCache["shallow_gdscript_cache<br/>HashMap&lt;String, Ref&lt;GDScript&gt;&gt;"]
    Cache --> FullCache["full_gdscript_cache<br/>HashMap&lt;String, Ref&lt;GDScript&gt;&gt;"]
    
    ParserRef["GDScriptParserRef"]
    ParserRef --> Parser["GDScriptParser*"]
    ParserRef --> Analyzer["GDScriptAnalyzer*"]
    ParserRef --> Status["Status enum:<br/>EMPTY, PARSED,<br/>INHERITANCE_SOLVED,<br/>INTERFACE_SOLVED,<br/>FULLY_SOLVED"]
    
    ParserCache -.contains.-> ParserRef
```

### GDScriptParserRef

The `GDScriptParserRef` class tracks parsing progress through status levels:

1. **EMPTY** - Not yet parsed
2. **PARSED** - AST generated
3. **INHERITANCE_SOLVED** - Base classes resolved
4. **INTERFACE_SOLVED** - Member signatures resolved
5. **FULLY_SOLVED** - Complete analysis done

Scripts can request elevation to a specific status via `raise_status()`, which triggers only the necessary analysis phases.

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_cache.h:41-120](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_cache.cpp:41-112]()

### Cache Operations

Key cache functions:

- `get_parser()` - Returns parser at specified status level
- `get_shallow_script()` - Returns script without full compilation
- `get_full_script()` - Returns fully compiled script
- `get_cached_script()` - Checks cache without loading

The cache handles:
- **Circular dependencies** - Detected during inheritance resolution
- **Status promotion** - Incremental analysis as needed
- **Source change detection** - Via source code hashing
- **Resource cleanup** - Clearing invalid entries

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_cache.cpp:113-500]()

## GDScript Class Structure

The `GDScript` class represents a compiled script.

### GDScript Components

```mermaid
graph TB
    GDScript["GDScript"]
    
    GDScript --> Native["native<br/>(Ref&lt;GDScriptNativeClass&gt;)"]
    GDScript --> Base["base<br/>(Ref&lt;GDScript&gt;)"]
    GDScript --> Owner["_owner<br/>(parent GDScript*)"]
    
    GDScript --> Members["member_indices<br/>(variable metadata)"]
    GDScript --> StaticVars["static_variables<br/>(static variable values)"]
    GDScript --> Constants["constants<br/>(HashMap)"]
    GDScript --> Functions["member_functions<br/>(HashMap&lt;StringName, GDScriptFunction*&gt;)"]
    GDScript --> Subclasses["subclasses<br/>(HashMap&lt;StringName, Ref&lt;GDScript&gt;&gt;)"]
    GDScript --> Signals["_signals<br/>(signal definitions)"]
    
    GDScript --> Initializer["initializer<br/>(constructor function)"]
    GDScript --> ImplicitInit["implicit_initializer<br/>(implicit constructor)"]
    GDScript --> StaticInit["static_initializer<br/>(static initializer)"]
    
    GDScript --> Source["source<br/>(source code)"]
    GDScript --> Path["path<br/>(file path)"]
    GDScript --> GlobalName["global_name<br/>(class_name)"]
```

**Key Members:**

| Member | Type | Purpose |
|--------|------|---------|
| `member_indices` | `HashMap<StringName, MemberInfo>` | Variable locations and types |
| `member_functions` | `HashMap<StringName, GDScriptFunction*>` | Compiled functions |
| `constants` | `HashMap<StringName, Variant>` | Constant values |
| `initializer` | `GDScriptFunction*` | User-defined constructor |
| `implicit_initializer` | `GDScriptFunction*` | Generated member initialization |
| `static_initializer` | `GDScriptFunction*` | Static variable initialization |

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:60-340](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:1-500]()

### Script Instantiation

Creating a script instance follows this sequence:

1. **`GDScript::_new()`** - Entry point for instantiation
2. Create native base object (e.g., `Node`, `RefCounted`)
3. **`GDScript::_create_instance()`** - Create `GDScriptInstance`
4. **`_super_implicit_constructor()`** - Initialize base class members
5. Call `initializer` (user's `_init()` if defined)
6. Attach instance to owner object

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:124-252]()

## Integration with Engine

GDScript integrates with the engine through the `ScriptLanguage` interface.

### GDScriptLanguage

The `GDScriptLanguage` singleton manages all GDScript operations:

```mermaid
graph TB
    Lang["GDScriptLanguage<br/>(singleton)"]
    
    Lang --> ScriptList["script_list<br/>(all loaded scripts)"]
    Lang --> Instances["script_instances<br/>(all active instances)"]
    Lang --> GlobalMap["_global_map<br/>(global variables)"]
    Lang --> GlobalArray["_global_array<br/>(global values)"]
    
    Lang --> Validation["validate()<br/>(parse and analyze)"]
    Lang --> Completion["complete_code()<br/>(IDE support)"]
    Lang --> Debug["debug_get_stack_level_*()<br/>(debugger support)"]
    
    Lang --> CallStack["_call_stack<br/>(execution stack)"]
    CallStack --> CallLevel["CallLevel structs"]
```

The language provides:
- Script validation and compilation
- Code completion for IDE
- Debugging support (stack traces, variable inspection)
- Global variable management
- Script lifecycle management

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:457-600](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_editor.cpp:146-215]()

### GDScriptInstance

Instances connect scripts to objects:

| Component | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `owner` | The `Object*` this script is attached to |
| `script` | The `Ref<GDScript>` being instantiated |
| `members` | Array of member variable values |
| `member_indices_cache` | Fast lookup for member access |

The instance implements the `ScriptInstance` interface, providing:
- `call()` - Invoke script methods
- `get()/set()` - Access script properties
- `notification()` - Handle engine notifications
- `get_script()` - Return the script reference

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:342-455]()

## Summary

The GDScript architecture implements a complete compilation pipeline:

1. **GDScriptTokenizerText** performs lexical analysis
2. **GDScriptParser** generates an AST
3. **GDScriptAnalyzer** performs type checking in three phases
4. **GDScriptCompiler** generates bytecode using **GDScriptByteCodeGenerator**
5. **GDScriptFunction** stores compiled bytecode
6. The **GDScript VM** executes bytecode
7. **GDScriptCache** manages dependencies and avoids redundant work
8. **GDScript** represents compiled scripts
9. **GDScriptInstance** connects scripts to engine objects

This architecture enables GDScript to provide static typing with runtime validation, efficient compilation, and seamless integration with Godot's object system.

**Sources:** [modules/gdscript/gdscript_parser.cpp:1-870](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_analyzer.cpp:1-632](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_compiler.cpp:1-208](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_vm.cpp:1-5000](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_cache.cpp:1-500](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:1-500]()2c:T5fd1,# Script Integration and Lifecycle

This page documents how scripts attach to nodes, the creation of script instances, and the invocation of lifecycle methods (`_ready()`, `_process()`, etc.). For information about the GDScript compilation pipeline (parsing, analysis, bytecode generation), see [GDScript Architecture](#6.1).

## Script Attachment to Nodes

Scripts extend the functionality of nodes by attaching to them via the `script` property inherited from `Object`. Both GDScript and C# scripts implement the `Script` interface defined in `ScriptLanguage`.

### Script Property and Instance Binding

Each `Node` can have a single script attached. When a script is set, the engine creates a `ScriptInstance` that provides the runtime bridge between the node and the script code.

```mermaid
graph TB
    Node["Node<br/>(scene/main/node.h)"]
    Object["Object<br/>(core/object/object.h)"]
    Script["Script<br/>(core/object/script_language.h)"]
    ScriptInstance["ScriptInstance<br/>(core/object/script_language.h)"]
    GDScript["GDScript<br/>(modules/gdscript/gdscript.h)"]
    GDScriptInstance["GDScriptInstance<br/>(modules/gdscript/gdscript.h)"]
    CSharpScript["CSharpScript<br/>(modules/mono/csharp_script.h)"]
    CSharpInstance["CSharpInstance<br/>(modules/mono/csharp_script.h)"]
    
    Node -->|"inherits"| Object
    Object -->|"has script property"| Script
    Object -->|"set_script_instance()"| ScriptInstance
    
    Script <|--|"implements"| GDScript
    Script <|--|"implements"| CSharpScript
    
    ScriptInstance <|--|"implements"| GDScriptInstance
    ScriptInstance <|--|"implements"| CSharpInstance
    
    GDScript -->|"creates"| GDScriptInstance
    CSharpScript -->|"creates"| CSharpInstance
```

**Script Attachment Flow**

Sources: [scene/main/node.h:1-900](), [core/object/script_language.h:1-600](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:1-500]()

| Step | Action | Code Location |
|------|--------|---------------|
| 1 | User sets `node.script = preload("res://script.gd")` | [scene/main/node.cpp:1-3000]() |
| 2 | `Object::set_script()` is called | Inherited from Object |
| 3 | Script creates a `ScriptInstance` via `instance_create()` | [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:1-3000]() |
| 4 | `ScriptInstance` is bound to the node via `set_script_instance()` | [core/object/object.h:1-1000]() |

Sources: [core/object/script_language.h:1-600](), [scene/main/node.cpp:1-3000]()

## Script Instance Creation

When a node with a script is instantiated, the engine creates a `ScriptInstance` that holds the script's member variables and provides method invocation.

### GDScript Instance Creation

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Owner as Node (Owner)
    participant GDS as GDScript
    participant Instance as GDScriptInstance
    participant Base as Base GDScript
    
    Owner->>GDS: _new(args, argcount)
    GDS->>GDS: _create_instance(args, argcount, owner)
    GDS->>Instance: new GDScriptInstance()
    GDS->>Instance: members.resize(member_indices.size())
    GDS->>Owner: set_script_instance(instance)
    
    GDS->>Base: _super_implicit_constructor(this, instance)
    Note over Base: Calls implicit initializers<br/>up the inheritance chain
    Base-->>GDS: Return (error check)
    
    GDS->>GDS: _super_constructor(this)
    Note over GDS: Find applicable _init()
    GDS->>Instance: initializer->call(instance, args)
    Note over Instance: Execute _init() with arguments
    Instance-->>GDS: Return (error check)
    
    GDS-->>Owner: Return instance
```

**GDScript Instance Creation Steps**

Sources: [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:124-207](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:100-300]()

The instance creation process follows a two-phase initialization:

**Phase 1: Implicit Initialization**
- `_super_implicit_constructor()` recursively calls implicit initializers up the inheritance chain
- Initializes default member values without parameters
- Processes base classes before derived classes

**Phase 2: Explicit Initialization**
- `_super_constructor()` finds the first applicable `_init()` method in the inheritance chain
- Calls `_init()` with the provided constructor arguments
- Only one `_init()` is called (the first found going up the hierarchy)

Sources: [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:124-207]()

### Member Storage and Indexing

GDScriptInstance stores members in a flat array indexed by `MemberInfo`:

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "GDScriptInstance"
        Members["members: Vector&lt;Variant&gt;"]
    end
    
    subgraph "GDScript"
        MemberIndices["member_indices: HashMap&lt;StringName, MemberInfo&gt;"]
    end
    
    subgraph "MemberInfo Structure"
        Index["index: int"]
        DataType["data_type: GDScriptDataType"]
        Getter["getter: StringName"]
        Setter["setter: StringName"]
    end
    
    MemberIndices -->|"provides index for"| Members
    MemberIndices --> Index
    Index --> Members
```

**Member Access Pattern**

Sources: [modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:250-280](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:500-600]()

| Operation | Implementation | Location |
|-----------|----------------|----------|
| Get member | `members[member_indices[name].index]` | [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:500-600]() |
| Set member | `members[member_indices[name].index] = value` | [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:500-600]() |
| Property setter | Call setter function if defined | [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:500-600]() |
| Property getter | Call getter function if defined | [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:500-600]() |

Sources: [modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:250-280]()

### C# Script Instance Creation

C# scripts follow a similar pattern but use managed objects:

```mermaid
graph TB
    CSharpScript["CSharpScript"]
    CSharpInstance["CSharpInstance"]
    ManagedCallable["Managed GCHandle"]
    DotNetObject[".NET Object Instance"]
    
    CSharpScript -->|"instance_create()"| CSharpInstance
    CSharpInstance -->|"gchandle"| ManagedCallable
    ManagedCallable -->|"references"| DotNetObject
    
    CSharpInstance -->|"Script Binding"| ScriptBinding["CSharpScriptBinding"]
    ScriptBinding -->|"registered in"| CSharpLanguage["CSharpLanguage::script_bindings"]
```

**C# Instance Binding**

Sources: [modules/mono/csharp_script.cpp:1-3000](), [modules/mono/csharp_script.h:1-600]()

The C# binding maintains a `CSharpScriptBinding` that holds:
- `gchandle`: GCHandle to the managed object (prevents garbage collection)
- `owner`: Pointer to the native node
- `type_name`: C# class name

Sources: [modules/mono/csharp_script.h:200-300]()

## Lifecycle Method Invocation

Nodes with scripts receive lifecycle notifications that trigger corresponding virtual methods. These methods are called at specific points in the node's lifetime.

### Lifecycle Sequence

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant ST as SceneTree
    participant Node as Node
    participant SI as ScriptInstance
    participant Script as Script Code
    
    Note over ST,Script: Node added to tree
    ST->>Node: add_child(node)
    Node->>Node: _propagate_enter_tree()
    Node->>Node: notification(NOTIFICATION_ENTER_TREE)
    Node->>SI: GDVIRTUAL_CALL(_enter_tree)
    SI->>Script: _enter_tree()
    Script-->>SI: Return
    Node->>Node: emit_signal("tree_entered")
    
    Note over ST,Script: Ready propagation (children first)
    Node->>Node: _propagate_ready()
    Node->>Node: notification(NOTIFICATION_POST_ENTER_TREE)
    Node->>Node: notification(NOTIFICATION_READY)
    Node->>SI: GDVIRTUAL_CALL(_ready)
    SI->>Script: _ready()
    Script-->>SI: Return
    Node->>Node: emit_signal("ready")
    
    Note over ST,Script: Process loop
    loop Every Frame
        ST->>Node: notification(NOTIFICATION_PROCESS)
        Node->>SI: GDVIRTUAL_CALL(_process, delta)
        SI->>Script: _process(delta)
        Script-->>SI: Return
    end
    
    loop Every Physics Frame
        ST->>Node: notification(NOTIFICATION_PHYSICS_PROCESS)
        Node->>SI: GDVIRTUAL_CALL(_physics_process, delta)
        SI->>Script: _physics_process(delta)
        Script-->>SI: Return
    end
    
    Note over ST,Script: Node removed from tree
    ST->>Node: remove_child(node)
    Node->>Node: emit_signal("tree_exiting")
    Node->>SI: GDVIRTUAL_CALL(_exit_tree)
    SI->>Script: _exit_tree()
    Script-->>SI: Return
    Node->>Node: notification(NOTIFICATION_EXIT_TREE)
    Node->>Node: emit_signal("tree_exited")
```

**Lifecycle Methods Table**

Sources: [scene/main/node.cpp:68-323](), [scene/main/node.h:400-500]()

| Method | Notification | When Called | Order |
|--------|-------------|-------------|-------|
| `_enter_tree()` | `NOTIFICATION_ENTER_TREE` | Node enters SceneTree | Parent before children |
| `_ready()` | `NOTIFICATION_READY` | All nodes in subtree have entered tree | Children before parent |
| `_process(delta)` | `NOTIFICATION_PROCESS` | Every frame (if enabled) | SceneTree process order |
| `_physics_process(delta)` | `NOTIFICATION_PHYSICS_PROCESS` | Fixed timestep (if enabled) | SceneTree physics process order |
| `_exit_tree()` | `NOTIFICATION_EXIT_TREE` | Node exits SceneTree | Children before parent |

Sources: [scene/main/node.cpp:68-323]()

### Ready Propagation Details

The `_ready()` callback is unique in that it's called in reverse order (children before parents):

```mermaid
graph TB
    Root["Root Node"]
    ChildA["Child A"]
    ChildB["Child B"]
    GrandchildA1["Grandchild A1"]
    GrandchildA2["Grandchild A2"]
    
    Root --> ChildA
    Root --> ChildB
    ChildA --> GrandchildA1
    ChildA --> GrandchildA2
    
    Order1["1. GrandchildA1._ready()"]
    Order2["2. GrandchildA2._ready()"]
    Order3["3. ChildA._ready()"]
    Order4["4. ChildB._ready()"]
    Order5["5. Root._ready()"]
    
    GrandchildA1 -.->|"call order"| Order1
    GrandchildA2 -.->|"call order"| Order2
    ChildA -.->|"call order"| Order3
    ChildB -.->|"call order"| Order4
    Root -.->|"call order"| Order5
```

**Ready Propagation Implementation**

Sources: [scene/main/node.cpp:325-341]()

The `_propagate_ready()` method implements this pattern:

1. Iterate through all children and call `_propagate_ready()` on each
2. After all children are ready, call `notification(NOTIFICATION_POST_ENTER_TREE)`
3. Then call `notification(NOTIFICATION_READY)` and `emit_signal("ready")`

This ensures children are fully initialized before parents can reference them in `_ready()`.

Sources: [scene/main/node.cpp:325-341]()

### Process Callback Activation

Process callbacks must be explicitly enabled:

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "Script _ready() Method"
        CheckOverride["GDVIRTUAL_IS_OVERRIDDEN(_process)"]
        EnableProcess["set_process(true)"]
        CheckOverride -->|"if true"| EnableProcess
    end
    
    subgraph "Node Processing State"
        ProcessFlag["data.process: bool"]
        ProcessThreadGroup["data.process_group"]
        AddToGroup["_add_to_process_thread_group()"]
    end
    
    EnableProcess --> ProcessFlag
    ProcessFlag -->|"true"| AddToGroup
    AddToGroup --> ProcessThreadGroup
    
    subgraph "SceneTree Process Loop"
        TreeProcess["SceneTree::_process()"]
        ProcessNodes["Process all nodes in groups"]
    end
    
    ProcessThreadGroup -->|"registered in"| TreeProcess
    TreeProcess --> ProcessNodes
```

**Process Activation Steps**

Sources: [scene/main/node.cpp:256-282](), [scene/main/node.cpp:619-639]()

| Step | Method | Purpose |
|------|--------|---------|
| 1 | `GDVIRTUAL_IS_OVERRIDDEN(_process)` | Check if script implements `_process()` | 
| 2 | `set_process(true)` | Enable process notifications |
| 3 | `_add_to_process_thread_group()` | Add node to process group |
| 4 | SceneTree calls `notification(NOTIFICATION_PROCESS)` | Trigger on each frame |
| 5 | Node calls `GDVIRTUAL_CALL(_process, delta)` | Invoke script method |

The same pattern applies to `_physics_process()` with `set_physics_process(true)`.

Sources: [scene/main/node.cpp:256-282](), [scene/main/node.cpp:619-639]()

## Virtual Method Call Mechanism (GDVIRTUAL)

Godot uses the `GDVIRTUAL` system to dispatch calls from native code to script implementations. This system bridges C++ virtual methods with script methods.

### GDVIRTUAL Macro System

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Node Class Definition (node.h)"
        VirtualDecl["GDVIRTUAL0(_ready)<br/>GDVIRTUAL1(_process, double)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Macro Expansion"
        VirtualStruct["struct {<br/>  StringName name;<br/>  bool valid;<br/>  uint32_t hash;<br/>} _gdvirtual_##name"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Runtime Check"
        IsOverridden["GDVIRTUAL_IS_OVERRIDDEN(method)"]
        CheckValid["_gdvirtual_##method.valid"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Method Invocation"
        VirtualCall["GDVIRTUAL_CALL(method, args...)"]
        CallScriptInstance["script_instance->call(method_name, args)"]
        ExecuteScript["Script-side implementation"]
    end
    
    VirtualDecl --> VirtualStruct
    VirtualStruct --> IsOverridden
    IsOverridden --> CheckValid
    
    CheckValid -->|"if valid"| VirtualCall
    VirtualCall --> CallScriptInstance
    CallScriptInstance --> ExecuteScript
```

**GDVIRTUAL Method Declaration**

Sources: [scene/main/node.h:400-600](), [core/object/gdvirtual.gen.h:1-500]()

The `GDVIRTUAL` macros create metadata for each virtual method:

- `GDVIRTUAL0(name)`: Virtual method with no parameters
- `GDVIRTUAL1(name, type1)`: Virtual method with 1 parameter
- `GDVIRTUAL2(name, type1, type2)`: Virtual method with 2 parameters

Example from Node:
```cpp
GDVIRTUAL0(_enter_tree)
GDVIRTUAL0(_exit_tree)
GDVIRTUAL0(_ready)
GDVIRTUAL1(_process, double)
GDVIRTUAL1(_physics_process, double)
```

Sources: [scene/main/node.h:400-600]()

### Call Dispatch Process

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Node as Node C++ Code
    participant GDVIRTUAL as GDVIRTUAL System
    participant SI as ScriptInstance
    participant GDScript as GDScript Method
    
    Node->>GDVIRTUAL: GDVIRTUAL_CALL(_ready)
    GDVIRTUAL->>GDVIRTUAL: Check if method is overridden
    
    alt Method is overridden
        GDVIRTUAL->>SI: call("_ready", args)
        SI->>SI: Lookup method in function map
        SI->>GDScript: Execute bytecode/managed code
        GDScript-->>SI: Return value
        SI-->>GDVIRTUAL: Return value
        GDVIRTUAL-->>Node: Return value
    else Method not overridden
        GDVIRTUAL-->>Node: Return default/null
    end
```

**ScriptInstance Method Lookup**

Sources: [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:600-800](), [modules/mono/csharp_script.cpp:1000-1200]()

For GDScript:
1. `GDScriptInstance::callp()` receives the method call
2. Looks up method in `script->member_functions` map
3. Calls `GDScriptFunction::call()` with arguments
4. VM executes bytecode and returns result

For C#:
1. `CSharpInstance::callp()` receives the method call
2. Uses managed callable to invoke .NET method
3. Marshals arguments to managed types
4. Returns result marshaled back to Variant

Sources: [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:600-800](), [modules/mono/csharp_script.cpp:1000-1200]()

### Automatic Process Registration

The Node class automatically registers process callbacks when virtual methods are overridden:

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph "NOTIFICATION_READY"
        Ready["Node::_notification(NOTIFICATION_READY)"]
        CheckProcess["GDVIRTUAL_IS_OVERRIDDEN(_process)"]
        CheckPhysics["GDVIRTUAL_IS_OVERRIDDEN(_physics_process)"]
        CheckInput["GDVIRTUAL_IS_OVERRIDDEN(_input)"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Automatic Activation"
        SetProcess["set_process(true)"]
        SetPhysicsProcess["set_physics_process(true)"]
        SetProcessInput["set_process_input(true)"]
    end
    
    Ready --> CheckProcess
    Ready --> CheckPhysics
    Ready --> CheckInput
    
    CheckProcess -->|"if overridden"| SetProcess
    CheckPhysics -->|"if overridden"| SetPhysicsProcess
    CheckInput -->|"if overridden"| SetProcessInput
```

**Automatic Registration Code**

Sources: [scene/main/node.cpp:256-282]()

This code in `_notification(NOTIFICATION_READY)` auto-enables callbacks:

```cpp
if (GDVIRTUAL_IS_OVERRIDDEN(_input)) {
    set_process_input(true);
}
if (GDVIRTUAL_IS_OVERRIDDEN(_process)) {
    set_process(true);
}
if (GDVIRTUAL_IS_OVERRIDDEN(_physics_process)) {
    set_physics_process(true);
}
```

This means users don't need to manually call `set_process(true)` if they override `_process()`.

Sources: [scene/main/node.cpp:256-282]()

## Language-Specific Differences

While both GDScript and C# follow the same lifecycle model, they have different implementation details:

### GDScript vs C# Implementation

| Aspect | GDScript | C# |
|--------|----------|-----|
| Instance Storage | `GDScriptInstance` with Variant array | `CSharpInstance` with GCHandle to managed object |
| Member Access | Direct array index via `member_indices` | Reflection/managed field access |
| Method Calls | VM bytecode execution | Managed method invocation |
| Constructor | `_init()` function | Class constructor |
| Inheritance | GDScript base class chain | C# class hierarchy |
| Type Safety | Runtime type checking | Compile-time + runtime checking |

Sources: [modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:200-400](), [modules/mono/csharp_script.h:200-400]()

### GDScript-Specific Features

**Default Argument Values**

GDScript functions store default argument values in the `GDScriptFunction`:

```mermaid
graph LR
    Function["GDScriptFunction"]
    DefaultArgs["default_arguments: Vector&lt;Variant&gt;"]
    ArgCount["argument_count: int"]
    DefaultCount["default_argument_count: int"]
    
    Function --> DefaultArgs
    Function --> ArgCount
    Function --> DefaultCount
    
    Call["Function Call"]
    CheckArgs["if provided_args < argument_count"]
    UseDefaults["Use default_arguments"]
    
    Call --> CheckArgs
    CheckArgs -->|"true"| UseDefaults
    UseDefaults --> DefaultArgs
```

Sources: [modules/gdscript/gdscript_function.h:100-200](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript_function.cpp:1-500]()

**Setget Properties**

GDScript supports getter/setter functions via `MemberInfo`:

- `setter`: StringName of setter function (called on assignment)
- `getter`: StringName of getter function (called on access)

When a property is accessed:
1. Check if `getter`/`setter` is defined in `MemberInfo`
2. If defined, call the corresponding function
3. Otherwise, access `members` array directly

Sources: [modules/gdscript/gdscript.h:250-280]()

### C#-Specific Features

**Instance Binding Lifecycle**

C# maintains additional lifecycle through `CSharpScriptBinding`:

```mermaid
graph TB
    Node["Node Created"]
    Binding["CSharpScriptBinding Created"]
    GCHandle["GCHandle Allocated"]
    ManagedObj["Managed Object Created"]
    
    Node --> Binding
    Binding --> GCHandle
    GCHandle --> ManagedObj
    
    NodeDeleted["Node Deleted"]
    ReleaseHandle["GCHandle.Free()"]
    ManagedCollected["Object Eligible for GC"]
    
    NodeDeleted --> ReleaseHandle
    ReleaseHandle --> ManagedCollected
```

**GCHandle Management**

Sources: [modules/mono/csharp_script.cpp:100-300]()

The `gchandle` prevents the .NET garbage collector from collecting the managed object while the native node is alive. When the node is freed:

1. `_instance_binding_free_callback()` is called
2. `gchandle.release()` frees the handle
3. Managed object becomes eligible for garbage collection

Sources: [modules/mono/csharp_script.cpp:100-300]()

## Summary

Script integration in Godot follows a consistent pattern across languages:

1. **Attachment**: Scripts are attached to nodes via the `script` property
2. **Instantiation**: `ScriptInstance` objects are created to bridge native and script code
3. **Initialization**: Constructor chain executes (implicit then explicit)
4. **Lifecycle**: Virtual methods are called at specific points via GDVIRTUAL
5. **Cleanup**: Instances are freed when nodes are deleted

The GDVIRTUAL system provides automatic method dispatch and registration, making it transparent to script users whether they're calling native or script methods.

Sources: [scene/main/node.cpp:1-3000](), [modules/gdscript/gdscript.cpp:1-3000](), [modules/mono/csharp_script.cpp:1-3000](), [core/object/script_language.h:1-600]()2d:T5403,# Resource Management

This document covers the resource loading, caching, saving, and import systems in Godot. This includes the `ResourceLoader` and `ResourceSaver` singletons, resource format loaders/savers, the resource cache, threaded loading, and the asset import pipeline.

For information about the base `Resource` class and its properties, see the Resource class documentation. For scene-specific resource handling like `PackedScene`, see [Scene Tree and Node System](#2.2).

---

## Overview

The resource management system provides facilities for loading, caching, and saving resource files from disk. Resources are loaded through format-specific loader plugins that convert file data into `Resource` objects. The system supports multiple formats (text `.tres`, binary `.res`, imported assets) and provides threaded loading capabilities for asynchronous resource access.

**Key Components:**
- `ResourceLoader` - Singleton for loading resources
- `ResourceFormatLoader` - Abstract interface for custom format loaders
- `ResourceCache` - Global cache mapping paths to loaded resources
- `ResourceSaver` - Singleton for saving resources
- `ResourceFormatSaver` - Abstract interface for custom format savers
- `ResourceFormatImporter` - Loader for imported assets with `.import` metadata

Sources: [core/io/resource_loader.h:105-311](), [core/io/resource.h:52-216](), [core/io/resource_saver.h:36-100]()

---

## Resource Base Class

All resources inherit from the `Resource` base class, which provides path management, caching, and lifecycle hooks.

### Resource Paths and Caching

Resources are identified by their path in the resource cache. A resource's path can be:
- A file path (e.g., `res://textures/player.png`)
- A scene-local path for sub-resources (e.g., `res://scene.tscn::SubResource_abc123`)
- Empty for transient resources not saved to disk

The `set_path()` method registers the resource in the global `ResourceCache`, while `set_path_cache()` sets the path without cache registration.

```mermaid
graph TB
    Resource["Resource<br/>(base class)"]
    Cache["ResourceCache<br/>(static registry)"]
    PathMap["HashMap&lt;String, Resource*&gt;<br/>resources"]
    
    Resource -->|"set_path()"| Cache
    Cache -->|stores| PathMap
    Resource -->|"path_cache"| PathStr["String path_cache"]
    
    GetRef["ResourceCache::get_ref()"] -->|queries| PathMap
    GetRef -->|returns| RefResource["Ref&lt;Resource&gt;"]
```

**Resource Cache Interface**

Sources: [core/io/resource.h:197-215](), [core/io/resource.cpp:79-116]()

### Resource UIDs

Resources can have unique identifiers managed by the `ResourceUID` system. UIDs allow resources to be referenced independently of their file paths, which is useful for refactoring and version control.

Sources: [core/io/resource.h:50](), [core/io/resource_loader.cpp:478-486]()

---

## Resource Loading System

### ResourceLoader Singleton

The `ResourceLoader` singleton provides the main API for loading resources. It maintains a registry of `ResourceFormatLoader` instances and delegates loading to the appropriate loader based on file extension and type hints.

```mermaid
graph LR
    Client["Client Code"]
    RL["ResourceLoader<br/>(singleton)"]
    Loaders["ResourceFormatLoader[]<br/>loader[MAX_LOADERS]"]
    
    TextLoader["ResourceLoaderText<br/>(.tres, .tscn)"]
    BinaryLoader["ResourceLoaderBinary<br/>(.res, .scn)"]
    ImportLoader["ResourceFormatImporter<br/>(imported assets)"]
    
    Client -->|"load(path)"| RL
    RL -->|queries| Loaders
    Loaders -->|contains| TextLoader
    Loaders -->|contains| BinaryLoader
    Loaders -->|contains| ImportLoader
    
    RL -->|"_load()"| Selected["Selected Loader"]
    Selected -->|"load()"| Resource["Ref&lt;Resource&gt;"]
```

**Main Loading Functions**

| Function | Purpose |
|----------|---------|
| `ResourceLoader::load()` | Synchronous load, blocks until complete |
| `ResourceLoader::load_threaded_request()` | Start async load in background thread |
| `ResourceLoader::load_threaded_get_status()` | Check async load status |
| `ResourceLoader::load_threaded_get()` | Retrieve async loaded resource |

Sources: [core/io/resource_loader.h:105-311](), [core/io/resource_loader.cpp:513-536]()

### Load Flow

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Client
    participant ResourceLoader
    participant Cache as ResourceCache
    participant Loader as ResourceFormatLoader
    participant File as FileAccess
    
    Client->>ResourceLoader: load(path)
    ResourceLoader->>ResourceLoader: _validate_local_path()
    ResourceLoader->>ResourceLoader: _path_remap()
    ResourceLoader->>ResourceLoader: _load_start()
    
    ResourceLoader->>Cache: get_ref(path)
    alt Resource cached
        Cache-->>ResourceLoader: Ref<Resource>
        ResourceLoader-->>Client: Cached resource
    else Not cached
        ResourceLoader->>Loader: recognize_path(path)
        Loader-->>ResourceLoader: true
        ResourceLoader->>Loader: load(path)
        Loader->>File: open(path)
        File-->>Loader: file data
        Loader->>Loader: parse_variant()
        Loader-->>ResourceLoader: Ref<Resource>
        ResourceLoader->>Cache: store(path, resource)
        ResourceLoader-->>Client: Loaded resource
    end
```

**Key Functions in Load Path:**
- [core/io/resource_loader.cpp:275-333]() - `ResourceLoader::_load()` - Main load implementation
- [core/io/resource_loader.cpp:477-486]() - `ResourceLoader::_validate_local_path()` - Path validation
- [core/io/resource_loader.cpp:538-642]() - `ResourceLoader::_load_start()` - Initiates load task

Sources: [core/io/resource_loader.cpp:275-333](), [core/io/resource_loader.cpp:538-642]()

### ResourceFormatLoader Interface

Custom resource loaders implement the `ResourceFormatLoader` interface to handle specific file formats. The loader must implement:

| Virtual Method | Purpose |
|----------------|---------|
| `_get_recognized_extensions()` | Return list of file extensions (e.g., "png", "jpg") |
| `_handles_type()` | Return true if loader handles a resource type |
| `_load()` | Parse file and return Resource instance |
| `_get_resource_type()` | Return the resource class name for a path |
| `_get_dependencies()` | Return list of external resource dependencies |

Sources: [core/io/resource_loader.h:47-95](), [core/io/resource_loader.cpp:62-223]()

---

## Threaded Loading

The resource loading system supports multi-threaded loading to prevent blocking the main thread during long load operations.

### Thread Load Architecture

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "Main Thread"
        Client["Client Code"]
        Request["load_threaded_request()"]
        GetStatus["load_threaded_get_status()"]
        GetResource["load_threaded_get()"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Thread Load System"
        Mutex["thread_load_mutex"]
        Tasks["HashMap&lt;String, ThreadLoadTask&gt;<br/>thread_load_tasks"]
        UserTokens["HashMap&lt;String, LoadToken*&gt;<br/>user_load_tokens"]
    end
    
    subgraph "Worker Thread Pool"
        WTP["WorkerThreadPool"]
        RunTask["_run_load_task()"]
        LoadImpl["_load()"]
    end
    
    Client -->|1| Request
    Request -->|creates| LoadToken
    LoadToken -->|registered in| UserTokens
    Request -->|creates| ThreadLoadTask
    ThreadLoadTask -->|stored in| Tasks
    Request -->|submits to| WTP
    
    WTP -->|executes| RunTask
    RunTask -->|protected by| Mutex
    RunTask -->|calls| LoadImpl
    LoadImpl -->|updates| ThreadLoadTask
    
    Client -->|2| GetStatus
    GetStatus -->|queries| Tasks
    Tasks -->|returns| Progress["progress, status"]
    
    Client -->|3| GetResource
    GetResource -->|awaits if needed| Tasks
    GetResource -->|returns| Resource["Ref&lt;Resource&gt;"]
    GetResource -->|removes from| UserTokens
```

**Threading Structures:**

| Structure | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `LoadToken` | User-facing handle for async load operations |
| `ThreadLoadTask` | Internal task state including progress, status, resource |
| `thread_load_tasks` | Map of path to active load tasks |
| `user_load_tokens` | Map of user paths to load tokens |

Sources: [core/io/resource_loader.h:129-211](), [core/io/resource_loader.cpp:337-475](), [core/io/resource_loader.cpp:675-718]()

### Load Task Lifecycle

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> THREAD_LOAD_IN_PROGRESS: load_threaded_request()
    THREAD_LOAD_IN_PROGRESS --> THREAD_LOAD_LOADED: Success
    THREAD_LOAD_IN_PROGRESS --> THREAD_LOAD_FAILED: Error
    THREAD_LOAD_LOADED --> [*]: load_threaded_get()
    THREAD_LOAD_FAILED --> [*]: load_threaded_get()
    
    note right of THREAD_LOAD_IN_PROGRESS
        Task executing in worker pool
        Progress updated incrementally
    end note
    
    note right of THREAD_LOAD_LOADED
        Resource ready for retrieval
        Cached if cache_mode != IGNORE
    end note
```

Sources: [core/io/resource_loader.h:116-121](), [core/io/resource_loader.cpp:337-475]()

### Cyclic Load Detection

When a resource being loaded depends on another resource that is already being loaded, the system detects this cycle and handles it by re-running the dependent task in the current thread context to break the cycle.

Sources: [core/io/resource_loader.cpp:812-893]()

---

## Resource Caching

### Cache Modes

The `ResourceFormatLoader::CacheMode` enum controls how resources interact with the cache:

| Mode | Description |
|------|-------------|
| `CACHE_MODE_IGNORE` | Don't use cache for main resource, use for dependencies |
| `CACHE_MODE_REUSE` | Use cached resource if available, cache new loads |
| `CACHE_MODE_REPLACE` | Use cache but replace existing resource's data |
| `CACHE_MODE_IGNORE_DEEP` | Don't use cache for main resource or dependencies |
| `CACHE_MODE_REPLACE_DEEP` | Replace mode propagated to dependencies |

Sources: [core/io/resource_loader.h:51-57](), [core/io/resource_loader.cpp:391-426]()

### ResourceCache Implementation

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph "ResourceCache (static class)"
        Lock["Mutex lock"]
        Resources["HashMap&lt;String, Resource*&gt;<br/>resources"]
        PathCache["HashMap&lt;String, HashMap&lt;String, String&gt;&gt;<br/>resource_path_cache"]
    end
    
    HasPath["has(path)"] -->|checks| Resources
    GetRef["get_ref(path)"] -->|queries| Resources
    GetRef -->|returns| RefRes["Ref&lt;Resource&gt;"]
    
    Resource["Resource::set_path()"] -->|acquires| Lock
    Resource -->|inserts into| Resources
    Resource -->|updates| PathCache
    
    Clear["clear()"] -->|acquires| Lock
    Clear -->|clears| Resources
    Clear -->|clears| PathCache
```

**Cache Operations:**
- `ResourceCache::has()` - Check if path is cached
- `ResourceCache::get_ref()` - Get cached resource reference
- `ResourceCache::get_cached_resources()` - Get all cached resources
- Resource registration happens in `Resource::set_path()`

Sources: [core/io/resource.h:197-215](), [core/io/resource.cpp:79-116]()
